Heavy Rain Washes Away Tracks in Eastern Shandong; Jiaoji Railway Interrupted

(Qingdao) According to reports, heavy rain poured down in various counties in Lu and Shandong, causing mountain torrents to erupt and rivers to rise rapidly. Several sections of the railway tracks between Zhangdian and Hutian stations on the Jiaoji Railway were washed away by the water at 11:00 PM on the 12th, interrupting traffic. Trains No. 1 and 2 running between Qingdao and Jinan were stopped at Qingzhou and Zhangdian stations, respectively. The railway bureau sent workers to inspect and repair the tracks, and traffic was restored at around 6:00 AM on the 13th. Train No. 2 arrived in Qingdao at 3:40 PM. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Qingdao) From 3:00 AM on the 13th, torrential rain poured down until noon, when it cleared up. The weather suddenly became hot, reaching 91 degrees, the first hot day of the year. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Jinan) Last night, a section of the railway track east of Zhangdian Station on the Jiaoji Railway was washed away by a mountain torrent. Trains going east stopped at Zhangdian, and trains going west stopped at Qingzhou. Traffic was restored this morning. (73 Special dispatch)

Xiaguan Water Level Stabilizes

(Nanjing) The water level at Xiaguan did not rise or fall on the 13th. According to records from the Public Works Bureau, the level was 6.86 meters from 8:00 AM to 12:00 noon. It dropped slightly in the afternoon. The water in the Qinhuai River has been reduced by about 5 inches after being discharged by water pumps. The dikes at Xiaguan have also been raised and thickened. If the water level rises by 3 feet, safety can still be maintained. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Hebei River Bureau Director Requests Dispatch of Troops to Patrol Dikes

(Tianjin) A Baoding telephone report states that the Hebei Provincial Government received a telegram from Qi Shou'an, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, reporting that the Shaanxi River has risen sharply, and heavy rain has continued for days without clearing up. Mountain torrents in the upper reaches of the Yellow River within the province have suddenly arrived, surging and turbulent, and the situation is extremely dangerous. There are many places where the embankments in the Shiche section are leaking and seeping, and the embankment body is immersed in many places where it is thin. River defense is extremely urgent. In order to prevent accidents, the director is personally supervising the workers day and night for emergency protection. However, bandits are stirring up trouble, and there is a fear of digging up the embankments to cause chaos. Please quickly dispatch a large army to assist the river soldiers in patrolling and guarding. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Yu Jichuan and Others Go to Yuan River Area to Survey Disaster

(Changsha) A great flood in the counties of Binhu, Changli, Nanhua, Anyuan, Yi, and Han has flooded millions of acres of fields and collapsed tens of thousands of dikes. Changli and Anyuan are the most severely affected. He Jian dispatched Yu Jichuan, the director of the Construction Department, on the 13th, along with members of the disaster relief committee, to survey the disaster in the Yuan River area. Xu Shiying, dispatched by the Central Government, will arrive in Hunan from Beijing on the 15th to survey the flood disaster. The provincial government has dispatched Cao Bowen, the director of the Department of Civil Affairs, to accompany him, and telegraphed the National Economic Council to allocate 400,000 yuan from the disaster relief funds stored in the Hunan Flood Disaster Association for emergency relief. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Shang Zhen Formulates Three Methods to Remedy Finances

(Tianjin) A Baoding telephone report states that Hebei's finances for the previous year had a total deficit of 6 million yuan. Chairman Shang Zhen has recently formulated three methods to remedy the situation: (1) Reorganize tax collection, (2) Stop military subsidies, (3) The monthly salaries of the provincial security teams will be paid by the central government. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Tianjin) A Baoding telephone report states that Shang Zhen said that the province's finances urgently need to be reorganized. There is currently a total shortage of 6 million yuan, and the original budget of income and expenditure is difficult to meet. The annual expenses of the courts are subsidized by the government by 1 million yuan, and the political expenses of the war zone are subsidized by the province by 2 million yuan. It is planned to present the deficit situation to the central government to request a plan for compensation. The funds from the military assistance branch in the province have been stopped, but it is planned to request the central government to reduce the subsidies for the courts and the war zone. He is now ordering the finance department to compile a new budget within ten days to ensure that income and expenditure are suitable. He is determined to entrust specialists to take charge of security, bandit suppression, and other matters in the war zone to facilitate command and deployment. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Qin Dechen Declines to See Guests Due to Illness

(Beiping) Qin Dechen has been handling affairs and negotiations in Chahar for the past month without rest. Yesterday, he vomited blood twice at his residence. After a Western doctor's examination, it was confirmed that a small blood vessel had ruptured between the eighth and ninth ribs on the right chest and was not a lung disease. He has now recovered and is following the doctor's advice to decline to see guests and plans to go to the hospital for rest. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Beiping) Matsui arrived in Beiping from Chahar yesterday. In the afternoon, he visited Qin Dechen with Takahashi, talking for about three hours to discuss the aftermath of the Chahar Province issue. Matsui went to Tianjin on the 13th to report to Umezu. Xiao Zhenhu arrived in Beiping from Tianjin at 6:40 PM last night. According to reports, he attended the farewell banquet for the committee members participating in the branch association and visited Qin to comfort him for his illness in the evening. Xiao said that the Chahar aftermath negotiations are proceeding smoothly and can be completely resolved soon. Song is recuperating in Tianjin, and his spirits are at ease. I received a telegram from Jiang yesterday with instructions and will not leave Beiping for three or four days. In other news, eastern Chahar is as quiet as usual. The Hitachi River Brigade in Gubeikou began to withdraw on the 12th and is preparing to withdraw in succession. In the future, Gubeikou will still be guarded by the Ishii Battalion. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Tianjin) Xiao Zhenying left Tianjin and returned to Beiping, and there is no date set for his return south. Zhang Yunrong, the chief of staff of the 29th Army, came to Tianjin from Beiping on the morning of the 13th to visit Song Zheyuan for instructions and will return to Chahar on the 14th. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Daming Society Bandits Incite Rebellion; Troops Encircle Them in a Flanking Maneuver

(Tianjin) The Daming Jinshengdao Society bandits, led by Zhao Dehuai and Feng Yuqing, counterattacked Longwangmiao Jintan Town at 10:00 AM on the 10th, engaging in a fierce battle with Guo Xipeng's troops of the 4th Cavalry Division for half a day, causing heavy casualties on both sides. A company commander of the 1st Regiment of the 4th Cavalry Division was killed in action. The two sides are still in a stalemate. Feng Zhanhai's troops of the 67th Army stationed in Pengde dispatched a unit on the 11th to arrive in Daming to suppress the bandits. The bandits are currently resisting stubbornly based on the terrain and inciting bandits in Chengan and Handan to unite and fight against the war. The army is having difficulty suppressing them due to heavy rain in recent days and obstructed traffic. About 200 Red Spear Society bandits, armed and equipped, were also discovered in Julu County, planning to attack the county seat and seize weapons from the tax police. The Handan and Quzhou tax police brigades have rushed to reinforce them. On the 10th, the 2nd Regiment of the 4th Cavalry Division stationed in Xingtai had arrived in Daming and, together with the 1st and 2nd Regiments, encircled the bandits with a flanking maneuver around the Wei River, Longwangmiao, east of Shizaozifang, and the Li Maoti west of the river. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Tianjin Japanese Military Statement: Suppressing Japanese and Korean Rōnin

(Tianjin) According to outside information, the Japanese military in Tianjin has issued a statement stating that Japanese and Korean rōnin who disturb the peace and order of North China have been suppressed. The China Youth League has been disbanded, and two Japanese members have been barred from entering China for three years, and one has been barred for two years. Six Japanese and two Koreans have been ordered to return to their countries. In the Kailuan mining area, some Chinese are impersonating people who have connections with the Japanese. It is being investigated. Now that relations between China and Japan in North China are improving, it is regrettable that these people are disturbing the peace. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Meng Clan in Beijing Hosts Feast for Three Sacrificial Officials

(Nanjing) Of the four Sacrificial Officials, Kong Decheng went to Shanghai on the night of the 12th, and the three sacrificial officials Yan, Zeng, and Meng are still in Beijing. At noon on the 13th, the entire Meng clan in Beijing specially held a banquet at the Meilichuan restaurant to entertain the three sacrificial officials Meng, Zeng, and Yan. Dozens of people attended the meeting. Meng Chuanqing, a representative of the Meng clan in Beijing, gave a welcome speech, and the Meng sacrificial official responded. The meeting ended at 3:00 PM. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

Sichuan and Gansu to Start Unified Tax

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance announced that with the imminent issuance of 30 million yuan in bonds to reorganize Sichuan's financial treasury, the foundation of which is guaranteed by the revenue from the unified tax and stamp tax on tobacco and alcohol, the commencement of Sichuan's unified tax is imperative. The measures for commencing Sichuan's unified tax have been prepared and are about to be announced. In addition, the Ministry of Finance and Zhu Shaoliang have agreed on the implementation of a special tax on cigarettes, and the tax collection measures will be implemented in Shanghai, where cigarettes and other goods transported to Sichuan and Gansu will be taxed in advance. Sichuan Province will only set up inspection or management agencies to prevent smuggling. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

Beijing Still Suffering from Extreme Heat

(Nanjing) Beijing continued to suffer from extreme heat on the 13th, with the maximum temperature still reaching 99 degrees Fahrenheit. The typhoon that occurred east of Luzon on the morning of the 12th has now moved to the northern part of Luzon and is still moving northwest, but the wind force is weak, and because it is a long distance away, the Yangtze River basin is not affected. Therefore, if there is no thunderstorm in Beijing, there is no hope for a decrease in temperature. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

Central Agricultural Experiment Station Continues to Recruit Agricultural Survey Reporters

(Nanjing) In order to investigate the national agricultural economy, the Central Agricultural Experiment Station has recruited more than 6,000 agricultural report reporters from various places, covering an area of 22 provinces and more than 1,200 counties. However, the distribution of these surveyors only covers half of the national territory. The institute has recently submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry to continue the recruitment in order to achieve the goal of one person per district in each county, so that the statistics on agricultural economics can be thorough and accurate. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

Ministry of Industry Orders Dispatch of Factory Inspectors

(Nanjing) In order to actively promote factory inspection throughout the country, the Ministry of Industry has issued an order to the construction departments of nine provinces, including Fujian, to appoint factory inspectors and instruct the personnel to submit their credentials to the ministry for verification in order to strengthen inspection administration. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

In the 24th year, a new mold will be cast, with a slight reduction in the circumference and an increase in the thickness. The Ministry of Finance's research results show that although the reduced circumference and increased thickness do not change the weight and fineness, it is feared that they may cause misunderstandings among the people. Therefore, it has been decided to use the original new coin mold to cast the coins, only changing the year. Casting of the new coins for the 24th year will begin after the completion of the 1st of August. (Special dispatch, 13th)

Soviet Russia Revises the Constitution, Stalin Takes the Lead

(Moscow) The Soviet Union has begun the work of revising its constitution. The most important aspect is the revision of the electoral law. In the future, all levels of Soviet elections will be changed to a secret direct ballot system. Although the Soviet Union has always adopted a universal suffrage system, the working class has enjoyed more favorable rights than the peasantry. For every 25,000 workers, one Soviet representative can be elected, while for farmers, it takes 125,000 people to elect one representative. After the constitution is revised, workers and farmers will enjoy equal electoral rights. Therefore, Chairman of the Council of People's Commissars Molotov stated that the purpose of this constitutional revision is to democratize the constitutional system. The Constitutional Revision Committee is divided into twelve subcommittees. Stalin, the General Secretary of the Communist Party of the Soviet Union, personally serves as the chairman of two subcommittees. Therefore, it is generally believed that the revised new constitution will largely come from Stalin's pen. (13th Havas Dispatch)

Russian Foreign Minister to Visit Czechoslovakia in Response to the Czech Foreign Minister's Trip to Moscow

Prague: Soviet Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov has accepted Czechoslovakia's invitation to visit Prague in response to Czech Foreign Minister Beneš's visit. The invitation was delivered by the Czech Minister to Moscow, but the date has not yet been determined, probably after the League of Nations General Assembly in the autumn. (13th National Telegraph)

Better Business for British Banks

(London) According to the half-year balance sheets published by the five major banks, business in the first six months of this year was indeed better than in the same period last year. However, doubtful debt continued to increase to £1,794,000,000, compared to £1,682,000,000 on June 30 last year, proving that the path to investment has not yet been broadened. Therefore, long-term investment continued to increase by £64,500,000, and doubtful debt to current accounts increased by approximately £19,000,000, but still only accounted for 41.4 percent of total reserves. It needs to reach 50 percent to be appropriate. Bills of exchange increased by £7,500,000, mostly due to an increase in commercial bills. Treasury bond reserves are trending downwards. Now that commercial demand is reviving, the Times raises the question of how long-term investments will be handled. The Times believes that banks will not massively sell their government bonds, as the large amount of capital required by industry seems to be met by the huge amounts of capital in storage. (13th Reuters Dispatch)

Current Commentary

Observations on the Authority of the League of Nations Amidst European Turmoil

— Heng

The turmoil in Europe has persisted since the Great War, but the unease and instability have been particularly pronounced in recent years. Besides Soviet Russia, there are two countries seeking stability in Europe: France and England. Their method of achieving stability largely relies on the League of Nations as the key to resolving all disputes. Therefore, restoring the authority and supplementing the strength of the League of Nations are necessary steps for stabilizing Europe. Since last year, as a result of French diplomatic efforts, there has been first the coordination between France and Russia, followed by Soviet Russia's entry into the League of Nations, which added a new force to the League after the withdrawal of Japan and Germany. This spring, there was also the establishment of the Franco-Italian Accord, which resolved the decades-long suspicions, jealousies, and open and secret struggles between the two countries in one fell swoop. The chaotic situation in Europe has also become significantly clearer. Subsequently, the Anglo-French London Declaration expressed a unified opinion on stabilizing Europe. By the time of the Stresa Conference, the diplomatic front of England, France, and Italy was even more unified. At the time, almost everyone who discussed the international situation regarded it as a major turning point for peace in Europe. Who would have thought that the authority of the League of Nations had not yet been fully restored, and the various agreements in the French bag had not yet been realized, and the League of Nations was again encountering serious difficulties. The contradictions in the European situation have also become more acute.

The reason why the current European situation has become more complex lies in the inability of England, France, and Italy to align their interests. The most obvious is the difference in the three countries' attitudes toward the League of Nations. In France's mind, the League of Nations is purely a tool to restrain Germany. Its purpose is only peace in Europe. As for whether the League of Nations has authority outside Europe, it does not bother to inquire. Italy, on the other hand, has never had a good impression of the League of Nations. The recent slight enthusiasm for it can be largely regarded as a gesture of gratitude to France. What it seeks is only to maintain peace in Central Europe. Apart from this, it does not need to rely on the League of Nations. Only England has a global perspective and wants to make the League of Nations an organization to maintain international peace. However, England is not without its criticisms. Although the three countries have different attitudes toward the League of Nations, they all take their own interests as their position. When the League of Nations can be used, they use it. If it hinders their actions, they treat it as nothing. For example, Italy indulges in its desire for colonies and openly opposes the intervention of the League of Nations. In order to maintain Italy's goodwill, France not only turns a deaf ear to Italy's actions, but also repeatedly prevaricates when England requests joint intervention, not wanting to offend Italy. Is this not a contradictory behavior of supporting the League of Nations on the one hand and undermining the League of Nations on the other? How can the establishment of the League of Nations be achieved in this way? As for England, the sudden establishment of a naval agreement with Germany this time, strictly speaking, cannot but be said to be a blow to the spirit of the League of Nations. According to Article 19 of the League of Nations Charter, the revision of the peace treaty must be approved by the League of Nations Assembly. Although Germany's rearmament is not entirely blameworthy, England hastily established a naval agreement with Germany without the consent of the League of Nations. From a legal point of view, it is not entirely consistent with the League of Nations Charter. It can be said that England's spirit of supporting the League of Nations is also inconsistent. Now, if it wants to occupy the position of leader of the League of Nations and intervene in Italy, it is no wonder that Italy retorts with sarcasm.

In short, among the major European powers today, there is no country that can absolutely abide by the Charter of the League of Nations and consistently uphold the authority of the League of Nations. Italy is blatantly undermining the League of Nations, and France is not wholeheartedly supporting it. England's attitude is also inconsistent. Therefore, as far as the current situation is concerned, the establishment of the authority of the League of Nations, the stability of the European situation, and the safeguarding of world peace are still far from reality.

Frequent Military Transport in Italian East Africa; 100,000 Italian Troops Have Crossed the Suez Canal, but France Has a New Proposal That Is Well Received: Abyssinia Under Italian Mandate

Asmara: Although Geneva still holds out hope that an Italo-Abyssinian war can be averted, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is sending a large army to Italian East African territories. The port of Massawa in Northeast Africa, which used to be deserted and extremely hot (reaching 120 degrees in the shade), has suddenly become very lively. Military supplies are piled up on the docks, as high as mountains, and heavy machinery is being unloaded from ships, including tanks, aircraft, heavy artillery, and mules and horses, all day long. There are usually four or five large cargo ships docked in the port, and they cannot unload their cargo because the docks are not empty. Water is scarce, and soldiers are limited to two pints. A major road is being rushed to be built through the mountains to alleviate railway congestion, as there is only one railway, just 120 miles long, and this is the only way to transport goods. The construction of the road is a great challenge for Italian engineers. Since March 27, 100,000 Italian troops have crossed the Suez Canal, and more will cross next month. Egyptian authorities are making every effort to cope with the congestion caused by the endless stream of troop transport ships arriving there. To avoid the heat, Italian soldiers remove their upper bodies and night clothes, resulting in several deaths from heatstroke. Donkeys and mules in Palestine, Cyprus, and Syria have been completely requisitioned. The docks and warehouses in Sudanese ports are also piled high with Italian war equipment. Arabs in Yemen, hearing of the high wages, are now flocking to Massawa to work. Meanwhile, the Abyssinian people are also preparing for war. According to London reports, large quantities of munitions are being unloaded in the Abyssinian capital of Addis Ababa. (13th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) France has now put forward a proposal for the Abyssinian problem. According to the Iraq model, Italy would be mandated to govern by the League of Nations. Diplomats here are considering this proposal. Abyssinia should have fulfilled the conditions of the League of Nations when it joined in 1923, but it has not done so to date. The only option is to treat it as a special case. According to today's news, Italy seems to be quite receptive to this proposal, but British officials are taking a cold attitude and not making any comments. If this plan becomes a reality, most of Abyssinia will be under Italian rule, except for the Lake Tana region, which will fall within the British sphere of influence, and the Addis Ababa-Djibouti area, which will fall within the French sphere of influence. If Abyssinia does not approve of this plan, Italy will invoke Article 15, paragraph 7 of the League of Nations Charter and has the right to wage war on Abyssinia. (12th National Telegraph)

League of Nations Secretary-General to Go to Paris for Negotiations and Meet Abyssinian Representatives

(London) League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol is scheduled to depart for Paris tomorrow (Havas, 13th).

(London) League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol recently came here to discuss the Abyssinian issue with British authorities. He is now scheduled to go to Paris early next week to report the results of the discussions to French Prime Minister and Foreign Minister Laval. If the prospects for negotiations are optimistic at that time, Avenol may meet with the Abyssinian permanent representative to the League of Nations (Havas, 12th).

(London) The governments of Britain, France, and Italy, as well as League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, are currently engaged in negotiations to find a basis for an agreement in order to convene a conference of relevant countries to resolve the Abyssinian issue. It is reported that Italy has not yet accepted this solution. Presumably, Italy will not accept this approach unless a basis for negotiation is established and it is favorable to Italy's demands. Avenol previously spoke with the Abyssinian permanent representative to the League of Nations in Paris. Therefore, Avenol must have a clear understanding of Abyssinia's views on the proposed conference of relevant countries. However, people at the League of Nations believe that there is a wide gap between the positions of Italy and Abyssinia, and it may be difficult to find a compromise (Havas, 13th).

(London) A solution to the Abyssinian issue is currently being negotiated by League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol, British cabinet members, and Italian Ambassador to Britain Grandi. It is reported that the purpose of the negotiations is to convene a conference of the three signatory countries to the 1906 treaty on Abyssinia: Britain, France, and Italy. The details of the negotiations are being kept strictly secret by officials, but it is generally believed that Avenol will not take any diplomatic steps before leaving London at the end of this week. According to the 1906 Three-Power Treaty on Abyssinia, Britain, France, and Italy agreed to maintain the political and territorial status quo of Abyssinia. In the event of internal disturbances in Abyssinia, the signatory countries agreed to adopt a neutral attitude towards Abyssinia's internal affairs. All actions by the signatory countries should be limited to protecting the lives and property of embassies and foreigners, as well as the common interests of the signatory countries. Moreover, even such actions must be implemented only after each signatory country mutually agrees that it is necessary. The three governments also agreed that in no circumstances should any of the three countries intervene in Abyssinian affairs without mutual consultation. If the political and territorial status quo of Abyssinia is shaken, the three governments agreed to maintain the political and territorial integrity of Abyssinia with all their capabilities. The convening of this conference of Britain, France, and Italy is probably based on the above-mentioned treaty provisions. However, the most difficult point at present is that Britain and Italy cannot agree on the boundaries of Italy's sphere of influence. Although the 1906 treaty generally stipulates the spheres of influence of Britain, France, and Italy, the boundaries of the spheres of influence are not specified in detail in the treaty (Havas, 12th).

Avenol's Speech: The Mission to England Relies on the League of Nations for a Stable Solution to Nationality Issues

(London) League of Nations Secretary-General Avenol delivered a radio address tonight, stating that if we return to the old ways and adhere to the principle of non-interference in international relations, there will be no hope for progress. His duty is not to negotiate, but to deal with various issues involving the League of Nations that are discussed by the governments of various countries. The main purpose of his trip to England is to meet with British Foreign Secretary Hoare and discuss with Prime Minister Baldwin and Eden some of the events that the League of Nations has experienced. Countries have a need to find a more stable method of international resolution on a common basis, and the League of Nations is the one that can truly represent the opinions of these countries. We must not be disappointed because the League of Nations has suffered a setback, and we must not forget the achievements that the League of Nations has already made, because the League of Nations has shown that it can adapt to current needs (Reuters, 12th).

The Main Theme of the US Meetings with Britain, France, and Italy

(Washington) According to reliable sources, Secretary of State Hull's repeated meetings with the ambassadors of Britain, France, and Italy have as one of their main purposes to express the United States' concern about the list of contraband that Italy and Abyssinia intend to issue in the event of war, so that neutral countries can abide by it. Today, a senator claimed that a similar situation existed from 1914 to 1916, hindering American shipping and ultimately leading to the United States joining the war. This time, the US government will clearly state that it has decided its own policy in advance regarding what goods can be supplied to belligerents, and will not allow others to make plans on its behalf. After talking with the ambassadors of Britain, France, and Italy today, Secretary Hull issued a relevant statement to reporters, reiterating the United States' faith in the Kellogg-Briand Pact, saying that this pact is still binding and is no different from when it was signed. The United States and other countries all want to maintain this pact and the dignity of the international obligations undertaken to promote and maintain peace among all countries in the world (Reuters, 12th).

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull attended a press conference yesterday. When asked about the United States' attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian dispute, Hull replied, "The obligations of the Paris Peace Pact are still valid today, and are no different from when 63 governments signed the pact. According to the pact, the signatory governments oppose the resolution of international disputes by war. The United States, like other signatory countries, wishes to see the pact respected and, in particular, wishes its obligations to be observed by the signatory countries" (Havas, 13th).

(London) It was learned here today that Britain and the United States have decided to cooperate on the departure of foreign residents from Abyssinia in the event of war in Africa (National Telegram, 12th).

Marseille George (given name) Hanson (surname), the US Chargé d'Affaires in the capital of Abyssinia, recently boarded a ship here to take up his post. According to his remarks to the press, "The United States is adopting a spectator attitude towards the Italian-Abyssinian dispute and is paying attention to the development of the situation. There is still no intention to change this attitude at this time. The United States is particularly concerned about the economic development of Abyssinia. The United States may be entrusted by the Abyssinian government to build sluices on the Nile River. As for my first task after taking office, it will be to protect the safety of overseas Chinese. There are three embassy staff members, one hundred and ten missionaries, and twelve black people among the Americans in Abyssinia" (Havas, 12th).

(Rome) The authorities here announced today that Secretary of State Hull's attention to the Italian-Abyssinian issue is unwelcome and unnecessary. They were surprised that Hull previously stated that this dispute had nothing to do with the United States, but now expressed a change of tune to the Italian Ambassador to the United States, Rosso. They were very impressed with the speech delivered by British Foreign Secretary Hoare to the House of Commons yesterday (National Telegram, 12th).

Italian Side Announces New Incidents

(Rome) The semi-official Stefani news agency released a message stating that there have been disputes in Qeymebayt, on the Italian-Abyssinian border. The following three incidents are among the most recent: (1) Two Somali herdsmen belonging to Italy drove their cattle herd to an area near Qeygora, inadvertently crossing the border and entering Abyssinian territory. They were detained by Abyssinian soldiers, who demanded a tax of four Thalers (currency name) per head of livestock. Because the two herdsmen were unable to pay, the Abyssinian soldiers confiscated the cattle and beat the herdsmen. (2) The Abyssinian authorities in the Adua area arrested 25 people one after another because they had sold food to the Italian consul there. (3) The wife of an Italian consul was traveling with a camel caravan to Eritrea when she was detained by Abyssinian soldiers in the Gonda district and held for one day. She was released after the consul protested (Havas, 12th).

German Lemon Shortage Due to East African Affairs

(Berlin) Germany is experiencing a large shortage of lemons, due to the large consumption of lemons by Italian troops in East Africa and the poor lemon harvest in Italy. As a result, prices in Germany have risen. According to the Price Control Committee, Germans should use German fruit acid as a substitute for lemons (National Telegram, 12th).

Red Cross Society Again Requests Membership

(Geneva) Abyssinia has not signed the Geneva International Red Cross Convention. Therefore, Abyssinia is not bound by respect for the Red Cross emblem, but it also has no right to fly the Red Cross flag to protect its battlefield wounded. The International Committee of the Red Cross has been requesting the Abyssinian government to join the Geneva Convention for several years without result. Recently, due to the imminent Italian-Abyssinian War, the International Committee of the Red Cross has sent a letter to the Abyssinian Emperor, reiterating this request. It is also reported that the International Red Cross has established a committee in London to handle Abyssinian relief matters. However, relief teams cannot fly the Red Cross flag unless they have been granted permission by the Abyssinian government. The International Committee of the Red Cross is currently working to find a way to resolve this difficulty, but everything will have to wait for a reply from Abyssinia before it can be resolved (Havas, 13th).

Austrian Prime Minister's Car Accident: Wife Dies Instantly; Deputy Prime Minister Rushes Back Upon Hearing the News

Vienna Austrian Prime Minister Dr. Schuschnigg and his wife were traveling by car for a holiday today when the car crashed into a tree near Landschloss. The car was destroyed, and his wife died instantly. Schuschnigg was hospitalized due to excessive shock. His daughter and a seven-year-old son were also in the car with the Austrian Prime Minister and his wife. It is not yet known how the car accident occurred. It is believed that the driver was momentarily dizzy, causing the car to crash into a tree. Everyone in the car was thrown out at the time. His wife died immediately. Schuschnigg and his children were fortunate not to be injured. The driver was seriously injured. A police officer in the car also suffered minor injuries. After the news of the accident spread here, the cabinet held a meeting. Deputy Prime Minister Starhemberg, who is currently on vacation in Venice, flew back to Vienna by special plane upon receiving the news. He will probably act as Prime Minister pending Schuschnigg's recovery (Reuters, 13th).

Romanian Authorities Decide on Joint Action to Deal with the Austrian Restoration Issue

(Paris) A correspondent for Le Matin claims that the authorities of Yugoslavia and Romania, when meeting at the Royal Palace in Romania, believed that the restoration of Austria was by no means a good sign. As a result of yesterday's talks between King Carol and Prince Paul, a common approach to deal with this matter has been agreed upon. Yugoslavia's and Romania's unease over Austria's trend towards restoration has become public knowledge. The two countries have also decided to take strict measures to prevent the realization of this plan. Furthermore, given that the Czech government supports the restoration of Austria, cooperation among the Little Entente may not be possible. Therefore, Romania and Yugoslavia may proceed with their plan independently if necessary (National Telegram, 13th).

Bucharest Yugoslav Regent Prince Paul arrived here this morning, but the exact time was kept strictly secret beforehand to avoid demonstrations. After getting out of the car, Prince Paul entered a waiting car and proceeded to the Royal Palace, arriving at 11:00 AM. He was welcomed by King Carol of Romania, Crown Prince Michael, Prime Minister Tătărescu, and the current cabinet members. After exchanging greetings, the entire group gathered in the floral carriage of Foreign Minister Titulescu, who had rushed back from London and Paris. Titulescu described the diplomatic and political situation in the carriage for two hours. King Carol then dined with Prince Paul, Prime Minister Tătărescu, Foreign Minister Titulescu, and Army Minister Angelescu at the Peleș Castle, and then resumed the meeting. Titulescu reported that he had informed the British government of the attitude of the Little Entente and the Balkan countries towards the Austrian restoration. Prince Paul plans to return to Bren, Yugoslavia, on Sunday to meet with Greek Army Minister General Kondylis, who is scheduled to travel from Rome to the area on Monday (National News Agency, 12th).

Sinaia, Romania Foreign Minister Titulescu recently visited Britain and France to discuss international issues and has now returned home to report the results of the visits to the cabinet and explain that the policies of the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente have remained unchanged. All of these countries fully agree to continue to promote this policy. Titulescu declared that the relationship is extremely important, because there are rumors that Yugoslav Regent Prince Paul's visit is due to the differences in opinion between the Czech Republic and Yugoslavia regarding the restoration of the Habsburg dynasty in Austria. It is said that Yugoslavia is strongly opposed to the restoration, while the Czech Republic believes that the restoration is the only way to prevent the union of northern Germany and Austria, and has expressed its support. Romania is in a difficult position between the two countries, and must decide whether to support the Czech Republic or help Yugoslavia. These rumors have now been denied by Titulescu (Havas, 12th).

British Emperor Inspects the Army, All Four Sons Attend

(London) The British Emperor and Queen inspected the army today, with all four sons in attendance. Tens of thousands of spectators watched. French Police Search Workers' District in Paris and Seize a Large Number of Rifles

(Paris) As a result of repeated searches by the police in the workers' district of Paris, a large number of rifles were seized from second-hand shops. The search was clearly to prevent incidents that may occur tomorrow, as left-wing and fascist groups are planning to hold demonstrations tomorrow. The situation in the entire city is extremely tense today. 20,000 police officers and a large number of police officers from various provinces have been dispatched to deal with incidents. In addition, the regular army stationed in Paris, with the exception of a small number participating in the parade, has been ordered to remain in their barracks (National Telegram, 12th).

(Paris) Tomorrow, Sunday, all parties will hold group parades to commemorate the National Day. The police authorities have banned private aircraft from flying over Paris on this day in order to prevent the throwing of inflammatory leaflets from airplanes. Although the police authorities have drawn up various preventive measures to deal with the clashes between left-wing and right-wing groups, they still feel it is necessary to prohibit foreigners from participating in the group parades. Therefore, they have warned foreigners that if any foreigners participate in the demonstrations, they will be deported once discovered. All police officers will be dispatched from tonight, Saturday, until Monday morning next week to prevent disturbances. In addition to this, in order to prevent occasional conflicts and unexpected incidents between left-wing and right-wing factions throughout the city, the national army has also been dispatched to maintain order (National Telegram, 13th).

French Submarine Explodes, Seven Sailors Seriously Injured

Toulon Last night, the French submarine Espoir exploded, seriously injuring seven sailors and several officers. Although officials have dispatched people to investigate the cause of the accident, the cause is still unknown as of this time (National Telegram, 12th).

Riots in Northern Ireland, Two Dead and Forty Injured

Belfast, Northern Ireland Riots broke out last night after the commemoration of the Battle of the Boyne. Two people died and forty were injured, including four police officers. Two factions of the police used bricks, sharp objects, and gunfire to fight fiercely in the streets. A police support team rushed to suppress the riots in armed vehicles, but to no avail. The police then fired warning shots into the air, but the crowd continued to fight fiercely. They then fired live ammunition into the crowd, killing two people and injuring several others, some of whom were seriously injured. One of the dead was a woman. During the height of the riots, someone fired a gun from the roof of a building on New York Street, and the police returned fire, injuring several people in the area. After dispersing the rioters, the police patrolled the riot area in armed vehicles. By 1:00 AM, the area was as safe as usual. The Battle of the Boyne was fought in the Anglo-Irish War in 1690, in which the Irish army was defeated (Reuters, 13th).

Heatwave in the United States, 63 Dead

(New York) According to recent estimates, the heat in various parts of the United States, especially in the western states, has killed a total of 63 people. 18 people have died in New York City. The temperature in the shade reached 91 degrees Fahrenheit today. Tens of thousands of residents slept on the beaches of Coney Island at night (Reuters, 12th).

Judgment on the Peking Union Medical College Hospital Lawsuit

(Tianjin) The verdict in the case where Ms. Ryder, an American residing in Tianjin, sued the Peking Union Medical College Hospital in the American court for neglect of duty was announced today. Therefore, cancer researchers around the world are constantly researching and experimenting, and cancer treatment methods are changing almost daily. The treatment given by the defendant was at least as good as what other hospitals in China could provide. Ma Zhanshan Accuses Ma Rong of False Accusation

(Tianjin) The Ma Zhanshan case continued to be heard on the morning of the 13th. Ma himself did not appear and was still represented by his secretary Du Xunruo, who brought recent photos to submit as evidence. Du defended the three items: 1. Ma Rong's lost son has a stake for hitching a horse behind his ear, while Ma does not; 2. Ma Rong is 51 years old, born on October 24th, while Ma Rong's lost son is 52 years old, born on the eighth day of the twelfth lunar month. Ma's original name was Zhenbang. When he became a battalion commander, Wu Junsheng changed his name to Zhanshan. Ma Rong's son's original name was Jinshan. The court asked Ma Rong whether he had any other evidence. Ma Rong insisted that Ma must appear in court for questioning. The court ruled that the evidence was insufficient and ordered another hearing. On the same day, Du Xunruo submitted a statement on behalf of Ma accusing Ma Rong of false accusation. After the court approved the statement and interrogated Ma Rong, it ordered Ma Rong to be released on bail. General observation suggests that Ma Rong may have a son missing. Because of his strong desire to find his son, he heard rumors and identified Ma as his son. The court may not prosecute him for false accusation due to his old age. Both cases are likely to be dismissed (Special Dispatch, 13th).

International Commercial Telegram—Special Commercial Report by Reuters, July 13th—

Gold and Silver

English Gold: The London gold price today is 140 shillings and 11 pence, unchanged.

English Silver: The London silver market is weak due to sales from the East. The spot price is 30 pence and 3125, and the futures price is 30 pence and a half, both down eight one two five. India, China, and speculators are all selling, but not much. The closing market condition is stable.

American Silver: The Mount Lyell silver market futures price opened low by about 150 pounds due to the fall in London prices. The market situation stabilized after the price drop.

Exchange Rates

British-American: Trading in the London foreign exchange market continued to be light this morning, with little price fluctuation. The opening exchange rate for British pounds against US dollars was four dollars, ninety-five cents and three seven five, lower than yesterday's closing rate by three seven five. The price did not change in the first hour, but rose by one eight seven five at noon, to four dollars, ninety-five cents and four three seven five. There was no change at the closing.

British-French: The opening price rose for the pound to seventy-four francs eighty-eight. In the first hour, it rose by three pounds to seventy-four francs ninety-one. This price remained unchanged until the closing.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market was sluggish today, without excitement. The price was slightly lower than yesterday's closing and remained stable. The weather is about to change, but merchants are still trending towards the short side.

English Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was also looser. The closing price for October futures was 6.24, down two pounds.

English Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was relatively slack this morning, showing sympathy for the American market. At the afternoon closing, the price for October futures was four shillings and nine pence one two five, down seven five from the previous closing.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened down one cent or so because the Liverpool telegram was unfavorable, and the weather in the wheat area is still good. It is expected that there will be more new wheat on the market next week, so the longs continued to close out positions this morning. The price of coarse grains was slightly higher due to strong demand for spot goods.

Securities

New York: When the New York stock market opened this morning, there was a strong market situation as found before yesterday's close. The stock prices of public utilities and bank companies remained strong because it is expected that the public utilities case will be revised, which will benefit the bank companies. Steel stocks remained strong because the automobile industry is expected to use more steel. Road stocks also appeared strong and attractive. The average price of Dow Jones thirty industrial stocks opened this morning at 122.34, up fourteen pounds. The prices are as follows:

Chairman Chiang's Speech on the Responsibility of Youth

—Attending an Enlarged Memorial Week in Chengdu—

Chengdu Correspondence: At 9:00 AM on the 8th, Chairman Chiang attended the sixth enlarged memorial week in Rong (Chengdu). It was held on the open space in front of the Zhigong Hall in the Royal City. Those present included Chairman Chiang, Secretary-General Yang, Director He, Chairman Liu, Army Commander Deng, Army Commander Liu, generals of various armies, representatives of various party and government agencies, various legal entities, various newspapers, and school staff, as well as the city's Boy Scouts, military training students from various schools, and all students taking the joint entrance examination, totaling more than 6,000 people. After Chairman Chiang led the participants in performing the ceremony as required, he delivered an impromptu speech as follows:

"Chairman Liu, respected principals, teachers, military training corps, and Boy Scout students, both male and female: Today, we gather everyone at Sichuan University for the Memorial Week of the Leader. This is a very rare opportunity. I, Chiang Kai-shek, am the Commander-in-Chief of the National Boy Scouts of the Republic of China and also the Chief Instructor of the National Military Training Corps. You Boy Scouts and military training students, as well as general middle school students participating in the joint entrance examination, are all my students, that is, my children. Therefore, today I have specially gathered everyone to tell you about the responsibilities you should bear and the cultivation you should have, and I hope everyone will pay special attention.

Now our country and nation are being invaded and oppressed by others, and cannot be independent and free, to the point of being in such a difficult and critical situation. What is the reason for this? You must thoroughly understand this reason, because you are the future masters of the country. In the future, how should we carry on the past, turn danger into safety, turn weakness into strength, and restore the independence and freedom of our country and nation? This responsibility rests entirely on you young people. Most people who are older now will die in twenty or thirty years, and the responsibility for the country and the world in the future will depend entirely on you to continue to shoulder it. If you can work hard in time, strive to become strong, and enable the country to be independent and the nation to be free, you can increase the glory of the country and nation, which is your glory. Conversely, if the country and nation cannot achieve a position of independence and freedom, and the country is eventually destroyed, you will become slaves and beasts of burden, suffering hardship and disaster, and your descendants will suffer torture for who knows how long. You must always remember that our Chinese nation, since its founding, has continued to pass on this beautiful land and noble culture to us. Now we have such a large land, such a good culture, and even more such a large number of compatriots. If we cannot save the country and revive the nation, carry on the past, restore our past glory, and create a new, independent, and free country to fulfill our great historical mission, then we have lived in this world in vain and have let down our Yellow Emperor ancestors and our parents. Therefore, you who will be the masters of the country in the future must take the world and the country as your own responsibility and take saving the country and the people as your only aspiration.

If we want to make the country independent and the nation free, first we should strengthen ourselves. That is, we must work hard at all times to forge a strong physique, cultivate a noble character, create rich intelligence, promote a spirit of tenacity and bravery, develop habits of hard work and discipline, and create healthy citizens of an independent country. With such healthy citizens, the country and nation will have a solid foundation for independence and freedom. With this foundation, we can then build a new country of freedom and independence, and then we can revive the nation. Secondly, if we want freedom and equality for our country and nation, we must sacrifice our personal freedom to seek the freedom of the country, and sacrifice our personal equality to seek the equality of the nation. We must contribute everything we have to the country and the nation in order to obtain the freedom and equality of the entire country and nation. If we individuals want to talk about freedom, the country and nation will be oppressed by others. If we individuals want to talk about equality, the status of the country and nation will decline, and eventually even the survival of the country will not be guaranteed. Everyone must know, what is the meaning of the so-called freedom and equality of the country? It means having a complete territory and sovereignty, independent spirit and national character. How do we sacrifice our personal freedom and equality to seek the freedom and equality of the country? That is, we must be able to strictly observe discipline and obey orders at all times and in all places. At home, we must obey our parents and abide by family rules. At school, we must obey teachers and abide by school rules. In the Boy Scouts and military training corps, we must obey the squad leaders, platoon leaders, and team leaders, and abide by military discipline and corps rules. In society, we must obey all levels of government and abide by all laws and regulations. Only when we can strictly observe discipline, obey leaders, and concentrate everyone's spirit and ability to serve the country and society can this country be considered a truly organized modern country. Only then can we generate overall strength to fight for freedom and equality, protect our five thousand years of glory, and in the future, you yourselves and your descendants can be true masters of the Republic of China. This is the most important principle of conduct and responsibility that you should understand. If you do not understand these principles and responsibilities of saving the country, it is useless to wear Boy Scout caps and uniforms or student uniforms. In reality, you will not be responsible for the future of the country and nation, but will be indifferent and complacent. Then you are not worthy of being a citizen of the Republic of China, let alone the master of the country. The above is about the responsibility of us young people in fighting for the freedom and equality of the country and nation, and in saving the country and reviving the nation. Below, I will talk about the position and responsibility that we as individuals, especially we young people, occupy in various different areas.

First, we must recognize our position and responsibility in the universe. When I teach faculty to enroll students, the first important thing is to tell them that the world and their parents gave birth to us, especially those who have become members of the educated class, about their position in the universe and their responsibilities. They must first understand this principle before they can be taught to become a good person. It must be understood that man is the most intelligent of all things, that is, the master of the universe, and we should give play to our intelligence and ability to understand the universe, control the universe, conquer nature, and utilize nature, and constantly create human culture. All things in the universe, whether sound, light, electricity, or force, whether moving, planting, mining, or other things, we must all be able to give play to our talents and intelligence to control everything, conquer everything, and utilize everything, so that the useless becomes useful and the harmful becomes beneficial. For example, when floods cause disasters, we must find ways to dredge them to develop water conservancy. When beasts cause disasters, we must eradicate or tame them. Our ancestors have paid great attention to the conquest and utilization of nature since ancient times. For example, Shennong invented medicine to relieve people's pain, the Yellow Emperor built palaces and made boats and carts, and invented the compass to facilitate living and transportation. Canzu invented sericulture to make silk, so that people had clothes to wear, and Hou Ji invented agriculture, so that people had food to eat. Dayu controlled floods, so that people could live in peace. These are all great achievements in conquering and utilizing nature to improve human life and create human civilization. Now, human civilization is advancing by leaps and bounds, and it is all due to mankind fully developing their innate talents and controlling the universe and conquering nature. Everything natural in the universe, in all its categories, is waiting for us to utilize it. There is no end to the new civilization of mankind, and it is all waiting for us to create it. In the past, our ancestors were very capable of developing their intelligence and constantly creating civilization, so our country was very strong in the past. Now, we descendants cannot develop our intelligence and continue to create new civilizations, due to the general rule of "if you do not advance, you will retreat," causing the country to fall into poverty and weakness, and the people's livelihood to become increasingly desolate. From this, we can know that if we want to save and transform the country and nation in the future, so that it can reach a realm of prosperity and strength, we must fully develop the inherent intelligence of our nation to constantly control the universe, conquer nature, and create new civilizations. In this way, we will not be ashamed of being descendants of the Yellow Emperor and citizens of the Republic of China.

Second, we must recognize our position and responsibility in the country. I have already roughly explained the position and responsibility of us young students in the country. You are the future masters of the country, and the responsibility for the rise and fall of the country in the future rests entirely on you. It can be seen how important your position is and how great your responsibility is. In the future, you must take the weight of the world and the country upon yourselves, strive hard, be self-reliant and self-reliant, earnestly take on the responsibility of carrying on the past, maintain the glorious history of our Chinese nation for five thousand years, and thereby promote and develop it, and create a country of the Three Principles of the People that is free and independent, standing proudly in the universe, seeking happiness for our 400 million compatriots, and establishing an indestructible foundation for our descendants.

Third, we must recognize our position and responsibility in society. You are all intellectuals in society, the backbone of society. Your talents and abilities are higher than those of ordinary people in general, and your circumstances are better than those of ordinary people in general, so your responsibility to society is even greater. What is this responsibility? In general, it is to labor and serve for society, and to seek benefits and create happiness for the people. In particular, we must do what is right, come forward bravely, and help the poor and suffering compatriots in general. One of the most important tenets of your Boy Scouts is "Do one good deed a day." This means that we must use the heart of loving others to extend our love to the general compatriots in society, and always do something every day to help others or benefit society, so that others and we can have clothes to wear and food to eat, without pain, and share happiness. This is the spirit of the ancients, "feeling hungry as if I were hungry, and feeling drowned as if I were drowned," and "regarding the people as my own children and treating all things as my equals." The ancients also said, "A scholar should be the first to worry about the affairs of the world, and the last to enjoy its pleasures." It can be seen that we intellectuals should be particularly concerned about the suffering of our compatriots in general and do our best to help them, so that we can fulfill our responsibility. Therefore, we must never only care about our own personal well-being and happiness, but must always remember the cold, hunger, and disease of our compatriots in general. As you have all seen, in Sichuan society today, there are countless displaced and helpless compatriots. As soon as you go out, you can see hard-working compatriots with sallow faces and thin bones, unable to push their carts or carry their loads, sweating like rain, and extremely exhausted, but they have to struggle hard to survive. How painful they are! We should help them at all times and in all places to reduce their suffering. You must know that foreigners, especially young students, will rush to help anyone who falls ill or falls on the road. If someone cannot push their cart or the cart overturns, they will do their best to help. If they see someone in trouble, they will do their best to help. They have developed this general spirit and habit of labor service. Now, we Chinese people are often the opposite. Not to mention those who have no knowledge, even you Boy Scouts and students receiving military training, I am afraid that few people can truly labor and serve society. Many people do not even labor at all. To give one of the most common examples, I see many students everywhere on the street, even Boy Scouts, who want to ride in rickshaws. You do not pull rickshaws for the elderly or serve society yourselves, and you have not fulfilled your responsibility. How can you want others to pull you? If there is no unavoidable circumstance, this is very wrong. You must know that a person born into society should take labor as life and service as his duty. If he is lazy and loves ease, he will become a parasite in society. If he becomes a parasite, he will eventually become a slave to a foreign country. We have been nurtured by society and should seek happiness for society. If we want to seek happiness for society, first we must be able to work hard and do everything ourselves. If we cannot do it ourselves, we should ask friends for help, and at the same time, we should do our best to help others at all times and in all places, especially to help our suffering compatriots in general. If we see someone fall on the road, we should help them up. If someone falls ill, we should rescue them. If the rickshaw pullers and those carrying heavy loads cannot pull or carry them, we should help them. These are the starting points for us to serve society and benefit mankind, and they are also the duties that each of us should fulfill to society. (To be continued)

Protecting Hankou's Zhang Gong Dyke Is Extremely Critical

Once Overflowed and Still Not Safe, the Whole City Is in Turmoil. All Dikes and Gates in Wuchang Are Leaking and Impossible to Defend. The Southern Section of the Pinghan Railway Is Three Feet Deep and Traffic Is Interrupted Again.

Hankou Correspondence: The waters of the Yangtze River in Hankou continued to rise rapidly on the 10th and 11th. As of noon on the 12th, the Jianghan Customs water level reached 50 feet and 8 inches. All dikes and gates in Wuhan are completely alarmed and the situation is serious, which is not comparable to a few days ago. Zhang Gong Dyke, the only guarantee for the entire city of Hankou, once overflowed due to the rapid rise of the Han River, which was higher than the dike surface, causing turmoil in the city. Fortunately, officials, civilians, soldiers, and police worked together to rescue it, avoiding a breach, but it was still not safe until late at night. Zhang Gong Dyke was built during the Guangxu period of the Former Qing Dynasty, and the project was very solid. Recently, the Xiang River has experienced a strange rise in water, and the pressure is too great, so it has become unsustainable. On the 11th, the water of the Xiang River was still three feet away from the dike surface. Overnight, the water suddenly rose by more than five feet, and the lower dike surface was one to two feet lower than the water surface. The water overflowed the dike at about 11:00 AM on the 12th, and the area around Boxue Middle School suddenly had a water level of more than ten feet. The Qiaokou and Shenjia Temple areas could be navigated by boat. The residents inside the dike were terrified, helping the old and carrying the young, and fleeing to the Pinghan Railway dike. There were more than 100,000 people, and boxes and belongings were piled up like hills. At this time, Wu Guozhen, the Mayor of Hankou, and Chen Xizeng, the Director of Public Security, were supervising the work on the dike. Seeing the water overflowing, they immediately ordered more than 10,000 laborers, together with the military and police, to stack sandbags to block the water. The water began to flow south over Nanyuefeng Bay and north over the Hubei East Automobile Road, entering the river through Chenjiaji. Zhang Gong Dyke was temporarily preserved. Zhang Xueliang, Qian Dajun, He Chengjun, Zhang Qun, Ye Peng, and others heard the news and went to inspect the dike. It was temporarily decided to raise the dike body and send a telegram to the Huangpi area to purchase a soil mountain, and requisition 170 trucks in the city to transport soil to Hankou, pack it, and fill the dike. On one side, the single-hole gate and double-hole gate were blocked to prevent river water from pouring into the urban area. When the dike was in urgent situation, it was discovered that twelve bandits were secretly digging. The military and police discovered this and immediately arrested them. Eight bandits escaped, and four bandits were arrested. It is said that they were immediately executed by shooting. It is said that they were instigated by a certain party and are being interrogated strictly. In the evening, the water in the Xiang River receded by several inches, but the dike was still not safe. Danshuichi and Chenjiaji were still leaking. There was a breach in the Huangjingtang dike. Water was gushing from the street center in Special Zone One, and rescue efforts were underway. Citizens throughout the city feared another flood and moved one after another.

Various agencies and organizations in Wuhan are now preparing for flood prevention. The Garrison Command has stipulated ten measures to order the garrison agencies and troops to pay attention to: (1) The command headquarters, special service battalion, and public security bureau in each district should send teams day and night to patrol the dikes within their respective jurisdictions to strictly prevent criminals from taking the opportunity to secretly dig into the dike body, and supervise their subordinates to work hard to help with the rescue; (2) If the dike breaches, the alarm bell should be sounded and gongs should be beaten to warn. The gongs should be beaten 30 times every five seconds; (3) If a certain dike is about to breach and cannot be rescued, or when the alarm bell is sounded, people living near low-lying areas should be quickly persuaded to move to the designated refuge. Those who hesitate and refuse to move may be forced to do so; (4) If the dike breaches and water floods the streets, subordinates should be supervised and ordered to work hard to maintain public order and traffic in the city, and assist in rescuing refugees. Strict precautions should be taken against bandits taking the opportunity to loot, and detectives should be particularly vigilant and pay attention to investigation; (5) If water floods the streets at night, and the power plant experiences obstacles, each should purchase lanterns and candles for backup; (6) For all waterlogged areas, collapsed houses, fallen power poles, or flooded power lines, the power lines should be cut off at any time to avoid danger; (7) The registration of people affected by the disaster should be designated to be handled by the Water Police Bureau. Citizens who need boats should be instructed to register with the bureau and obtain flags; (8) For all boats needed to perform garrison duties after the disaster, the chief officers of each garrison agency and troop should hire them themselves according to the necessary number, and report the list to the headquarters for verification; (9) After the disaster, each garrison agency, troop, police service, and hired boat should report a list for verification. In Wuchang, all the dikes are leaking. The main dikes, from Qingshan to Jinkou, were originally divided into four sections for protection. In the first section, from Jinkou to Baiguan, and from Wuxian Temple to Xiaojia Wharf, the river water was subjected to a large army rushing from the top, and the dike body was washed away and about to collapse. There were many leaks in the Zhoujiazhui and Yangsiji areas, which were impossible to prevent. The second section was from Baiguan to Wutai Gate, and the water flowing from the gate was very strong. The third section was from Wutai Gate to Xiaxinhe. Cracks were found in the Wuchang Customs Wharf in the middle, and the water was higher than the old dike. The fourth section was from Xiaxinhe to Wufeng Gate. The landslide was subjected to wind and waves, and most of it collapsed. Water overflowed in the Felt Factory area. Above Qingshan, it connects to the Wuhui Dyke, which is also one of the main dikes. A week ago, it showed signs of danger. Now the water level has approached the top of the dike, and there are leaks everywhere, which are really impossible to prevent. The inside of the twelve-day-old foot began to collapse, which is a precursor to collapse. In addition, the roadbed of Xujiapeng and the Huaguotizi dike outside the second section of the main dike collapsed at the same time. The Wujin dike is also extremely dangerous. If the water level rises again, it cannot be preserved. The Provincial Flood Control Association has determined a flood control plan. If the area from above Wutai Gate to Longchuanji collapses, the river water will reach the urban area directly. The Shaihu Dike Gate should be blocked, Xiangguosi Street should be raised, the railway gap at Tongxiangmen should be blocked, the Jinshui Gate should be prevented from being flooded, the sub-dike should be rescued, and it is hoped that the urban area and various districts behind the Wufeng Dike can be preserved. If the Wufeng Dike collapses, the railway hole next to Changchun Temple should be blocked, the Boxue Academy sub-dike should be built, the Binyangmen bridge hole should be blocked, Wushengmen Street should be blocked, Changsheng Gate should be blocked, and the lateral dike should be raised. It is hoped that the Wujin Dike in front of the mountain can be preserved. If the river water rises above 53 feet, it will be beyond our ability to support it.

The railway track of the Pinghan Railway that was flooded was repaired on the 11th, and trains heading north could reach Yancheng directly. On the 12th, it was flooded again. The water depth along the way from Chenjiaji in Hankou to Xiaogan was three feet, and all vehicles were suspended. Traffic was interrupted again. Only one train carrying soil to Hankou from Huangpi arrived, and it was blocked by water, so it could not continue to be transported. Raising the dike body of Zhang Gong Dyke also encountered obstacles. (12th)

Hubei Province: Establishment of a Disaster Relief General Association

Appointed He Chengjun and others as committee members; internally divided into six groups for office work.

Hankou correspondence: The Jiangxiang area is suffering from severe flooding. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed various provincial authorities, instructing them on relief measures. In addition to the establishment of a Disaster Relief General Association by the Xingying (General Headquarters) to oversee the overall situation, each province will also organize its own provincial Disaster Relief General Association. At 11:00 AM on the 11th, the Hubei Provincial Government held a preparatory meeting. Chairman Zhang Qun reported on the flood situation and the provincial government's approval to distribute 100,000 yuan for emergency relief. Subsequently, the method of organizing the Disaster Relief General Association was discussed. In addition to the provincial government, provincial and municipal party departments, and all committee members serving as ex-officio members, He Chengjun, Fang Benren, Xu Yuanquan, Xia Douyin, He Hengfu, Zhou Xingtang, Huang Wenzhi, Zhao Zhongxuan, Su Taiyu, Chai Yeyu, Zhou Shaoyuan, Liu Shaoyan, Xiao Zhichu, Zhang Wanxin, Rong Jingfang, Xu Rongting, Ye Peng, Zheng Xieqing, Zhao Dianzhi, Xi Debing, Tan Gongyuan, Chen Jingyu, Xie Fencheng, Nan Kui, Li Zuji, Fang Shaoyan, Pu Xinya, Li Dezhai, Gao Bochang, Shu Binyu, Zhou Cangbo, Wang Daoping, Huang Jiting, Yang Jiqian, Hua Dongchen, Liu

Huchen, Li Ding'an, Hu Zhichu, Wang Xiaocheng, Lu Fangcai, Huang Houqing, Chen Xianzhou, Yu Rongqiao, Tao Gongdi, He Wenbing, Yang Huiting, Yang Songtuan, Zhu Ruifeng, Lu Deze, Chen Yanjiong, Yin Deyang, Xu Ziqing, Yang Silian, Li Zikuan, Fang Dazhi, Ju Zheng, Wang Shijie, Shi Ying, Xiong Bin, Zhang Chengdao, Fang Juehui, Jiang Zuobin, Zhang Zhiben, Wu Xingya, Guan Jiongzhi, Han Yunqing, Zhang Nanxian, Kong Geng, Shen Honglie, Shen Zhaonian, Gao Yihan, Ren Yingzhong, Zhu Hengshui, Shi Yancheng, Zhang Qihong, Yang Kuiyi, Chen Guangzu, Jin Jutang, Chen Xizeng, Ren Hongjun, Zhu Chuanjing, Guo Taizhen, Wu Xianren, Ding Bingquan, Geng Bozhao, Peng Jieshi, Li Jiecai, Cai Mengjian, Chen Shi, Zeng Yiding, Yao Yuanlun, Zhang Xiang, Xu Weitang, Zhang Xiuchun, Liu Jucun, Wang Kaihua, Li Bogang, and Li Boren were appointed as committee members.
