Two proposals were also discussed: (1) Floating corpses washed down along the river should be salvaged and buried by various charitable halls, with expenses covered by the association. (2) The livelihood expenses of the rescue boats organized by the Water Police Bureau, at eight jiao per boat per day, will be covered by the association. (12th)

Qin Chuanzheng and Others: Report on Flood Situation Inspection – and Recommendations for Future Measures –

Recently, the Yangtze and Yellow Rivers have both seen a surge in water levels simultaneously. The great flood of 1931 is about to repeat itself today. People across the country are deeply concerned. It is reported that Qin Fen, Secretary-General of the National Economic Commission, Fu Rulin, Chairman of the Yang (Yangtze River) Committee, and Zheng Jujing, Deputy Director of the Water Conservancy Department of the Economic Commission, and others, inspected the water situation in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River. They returned to Beijing this afternoon (13th) and subsequently released a detailed inspection report and proposed future measures. Excerpts are as follows:

Inspection along the Yangtze River

(1) On July 6th, the commission received a report from the Jianghan Engineering Bureau stating that the water level at Yidu rose sharply by about eight feet on the 5th. The water level has already exceeded the highest flood level of 1931. The downstream embankments are under extreme pressure and are likely to breach, making rescue efforts difficult. At the same time, it was learned that private dikes in Anhui and Jiangxi were collapsing one after another. Therefore, it was decided to depart the next morning with engineering personnel to inspect along the Yangtze River. (2) Left Beijing on the morning of July 7th and arrived in Wuhu at noon. The water level at this port has reached 28 feet, only about one foot from the bank. However, in the areas around Yihua Wharf and the low-lying areas in the western part of the port, the water has already reached the shore. According to a report by Magistrate Gao Wenbo of the county, efforts are being made to protect the dangerous areas near the various dikes. Chairman Liu Zhenhua had come to Wuhu two days ago to inspect. In the afternoon, a small customs launch was taken to inspect the nearby dikes. The county magistrate was supervising local people to protect the dikes and was immediately comforted. At 7:00 PM, boarded the Gonghe steamer and sailed upstream. (3) Arrived in Anqing at 9:00 AM on the morning of July 8th and went to the Anhui Provincial Government to meet Chairman Liu to discuss everything. It was learned that in recent days, Chairman Liu had inspected along the Yangtze River and personally guided flood prevention in various counties, which encouraged the local people even more. As a result, within Anhui, in addition to a few private dikes that breached due to high water levels, most of the main embankments were preserved. Director Liu Yiyan of the Construction Department was on his way to inspect the breach at the Mahua Dike. In the afternoon, Chairman Liu boarded the Anfeng warship and sailed upstream. At 8:00 PM, arrived in Dongliu County. The city wall here was quite dangerous because both the river and lake levels had risen. Chairman Liu immediately ordered Magistrate Zhang of the county to lead the gentry and people to rush to protect it overnight and gave 500 yuan at the time to prepare materials. At 11:00 PM, temporarily docked at the mouth of the Huayang River. (4) The ship departed at dawn on July 9th and arrived at the breach of the Mahua Dike in Jiangxi at 10:00 AM. Inspected the dike. The breach was about 60 zhang wide. Inside the dike was a reservoir lake with a large area. Although the Yangtze River water was pouring in and very turbulent, the residents by the lake showed few signs of disaster and were not very serious. Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangxi have all sent personnel to work to find ways to protect it. Fearing that the authority was not unified and it would be difficult to achieve results, we discussed the dike blocking method with Chairman Liu. Since the land is adjacent to Anhui, it was recommended that Director Liu Yiyan of the Anhui Construction Department be responsible for the dike blocking, with Yang Committee members supervising and directing. The cost will be shared by Anhui, Hubei, Jiangxi as usual, and the central government will give appropriate subsidies. Thirty thousand yuan has been allocated first from the flood prevention funds to the Anhui Construction Department. At noon, we arrived at the border between Jiangxi and Anhui. Chairman Liu took another Anjie ship back to the province, and the Anfeng ship continued to send it to Jiujiang. By then it was 8:00 PM. The personnel of the Xunyang surveying team stationed by the Yang Committee were transferred to Mahua Dike to assist in everything. The water depth on the roads along the river in Jiujiang reached about two or three feet. The rivers and lakes inside were flooded. According to the report of Yan Fangtian, Director of the Jiangxi Provincial Water Conservancy Bureau, more than 100 folk-level areas in the Poyang River area were breached. The dikes of the Jiangxi Province along the Yangtze River are also extremely dangerous and need to be suspected of three to four thousand yuan before they can be protected. The director of the bureau was immediately ordered to summon civilians and do his best to protect them and allocated 4,000 yuan from the flood prevention funds for materials. At the same time, the Jiangxi Construction Department was notified to inspect it, asking it to supervise the flood prevention affairs of the counties to avoid negligence. Since Chairman Xiong had not yet returned to the province, and it was heard that the Nanchang-Jiujiang Railway was blocked by water and traffic had not resumed, at 9:30 PM at night, the Wusong wheel was changed to sail. (5) On July 10th, we sailed into Hubei Province. The main embankments along the river were still five or six feet above the river surface. Along the embankment, hundreds of workers dispatched by the Jianghan Bureau were seen implementing visit engineering. There was no breach. Arrived in Hankou at 5:00 PM in the afternoon. Director Liu Shoupeng of the Hubei Construction Department reported that the flood prevention situation in Wuchang was very Zhou. According to the report of Yang Silian, Director of the Jianghan Engineering Bureau of this committee, the main embankments below Hankou are still good, but the water level in the Jianli area of Shaoshi has exceeded the flood level of 1931. Slightly, there were three or four breaches, all of which were not important. The embankments in Hubei Province have been ordered to be closely guarded by the various engineering offices and to visit each place for guidance. The current water level in Hankou has reached 49 feet, the roads have not yet been flooded, and the banks along the river are particularly strong in preventing the floods. According to this water situation, the embankments in 1931 had already collapsed, and the city of Hankou was in the center of the water. Regarding the flood prevention funds, 250,000 yuan had been allocated from the dike works account of Hubei Province under the jurisdiction of this committee, which was still sufficient for use. The bureau requested another 50,000 yuan, which was approved and allocated. The director of the bureau was ordered to effectively protect it. On this day, at 6:00 PM, we took a car to inspect along the Zhang Gong Dike. The dike surrounded the city of Hankou, and the Yangtze River water was about a zhang higher than the fields inside the dike. The dike was surrounded on all sides. The dike was the key to the safety of the city of Hankou. The Jianghan Bureau has been building and repairing it for many years and paid special attention to it. A leak was found in the eastern part of the riverside a few days ago, which has been jointly protected by the bureau, the Xingying, the Pinghan Railway Bureau, and the Hankou Municipal Government, and it is safe to say that there will be no problem. Subsequently, we received a telegram from Beijing, learning that the Yellow River water has also risen sharply. The Ice Committee meeting is about to be held, and Director Mao Yisheng will also arrive in Australia tomorrow to continue the supervision. Then, the arrangements were made, some people were left in Hankou to assist, and Zhu Ercheng, Division Shi Jun, and Xi Rong were sent to Hunan Province to inspect. Therefore, it was decided to return to Beijing the next morning. (6) At 7:00 AM on July 11th, we went to the Xingying to meet with Director Zhang Xueliang and learned that Director Zhang had taken a plane to inspect the upper reaches and told us about the flood situation in Shashi and Xianghe, which was extremely detailed. At 10:00 AM, we left Hankou on the Gonghe to return to Beijing. (7) Recently, the water has risen, and navigation has been suspended at night. It was not until the morning of July 13th that we arrived at the Wuhu Wharf and learned that the water levels in Anqing and Wuhu have not risen or fallen much, while the water level in Hankou rose sharply again at 1:00 PM on the 11th, reaching a height of 50 feet. The embankments are becoming more and more dangerous, which is very worrying. The water level in Jiujiang also rose by four inches. At the same time, we also learned that the Yellow River water has also risen sharply, and the Linyi embankment in Shandong Province has breached. The entire river embankment is under pressure. According to the Yellow River flood, the highest level is usually in early August. This time, the water level is so fierce in mid-July, which is really unexpected. We will return to Beijing today to make arrangements and urge internal personnel to intensify their work day and night during the emergency flood prevention period.

Current Protection

The magnitude of the Yangtze River's water level is not much different from that of the 1931 flood. At that time, the dikes along the river had long collapsed and could not be salvaged. This year, the main dikes along the river have been rebuilt by the National Government's Flood Relief Association, and recent protection efforts have been strong. Therefore, no major breaches have occurred. Only in places where the water level is particularly high and human power cannot be saved, the folk dikes have been flooded. However, there are indeed many embankments that have been kept safe by rescue and protection. Recently, the flood season has not passed, and the water level in the upper reaches has slightly decreased in recent days. It is inevitable that it will rise again. The following is a list of the urgent tasks currently being undertaken: (1) The provincial governments should supervise local officials and people to guard the dikes in sections and work together to protect them. If the officials can personally inspect and provide guidance, the local officials, gentry, and people will be more encouraged and enthusiastic about their work, and more dikes will be preserved. (2) For the dikes that have breached, some of which have very strong water flow and the affected area is not too wide, it seems uneconomical to immediately plug them. The water conservancy organs should immediately protect both ends of the dike to avoid further expansion. Once the water recedes and the dike foundation dries up, the dike can be restored, which will be more effective and cost less. (3) In the areas along the river that have been flooded, only the tops of thatched houses can be seen now, and the water is level with the eaves. The people who have been displaced must be numerous, and during the floods, epidemics are easy to spread. Disease prevention is also very important. The provinces should immediately provide relief in accordance with Chairman Chiang's flood relief measures. (4) The local governments should immediately send personnel to investigate the flooded areas and detailed conditions within their jurisdictions and quickly report them to the provincial governments for forwarding to the Yang Committee, so as to coordinate the planning of the Yangtze River's flood control measures.

Post-Flood Measures

The Yangtze River is the most benign river in the world, but in recent years it has become a frequent source of floods. The reasons are very complex, but the most obvious is that the lakes and swamps that used to store water, as well as the beaches and sandbars along the river, have mostly been reclaimed into farmland, competing with the water, which will inevitably lead to breaches. This is common sense. Therefore, after this year's major flood, when the water level drops, there is an urgent need to coordinate remedial measures so that flood control can be carried out before the fundamental plan for the Yangtze River has been planned and implemented. The following are listed for selection: (1) The Yang Committee shall, according to the flooding conditions in various places, plan to reserve the area of lakes and swamps for water storage. Private dikes that are directly harmful to water storage must not be repaired. Detailed measures shall be negotiated and handled by the committee and the provincial governments. (2) The Yang Committee will survey the height of the dikes along the river, plan the size of the main dikes to be raised and thickened, and negotiate with the provincial governments to order local governments to carry out small-scale repairs during the agricultural slack season. The central government will provide appropriate subsidies when necessary. (3) After the water recedes at the breach of the main dike, the Yang Committee will send technicians to guide the water conservancy organs of various provinces to repair them separately according to the needs, so that they are legal. (4) The Yang Committee will send personnel to carefully inspect and plan the Yangtze River waterway and the lakes of various tributaries and formulate a fundamental plan for phased implementation.

Wuhu Area: Yangtze River Water Level Gradually Stabilizing; Provincial Government Still Orders Intensified Flood Defense

Wuhu Correspondence: The Yangtze River water level, which had been rising sharply for half a month, has gradually stabilized in the last three days. The Wuhu Jiangchao (tidal level) fell five inches from the 10th to the 12th, with the customs water mark receding from 28 feet 6 inches to 28 feet 1 inch. The river water flowing downstream is also not as turbulent as in the previous days. Although 30 to 40 good dikes along the Anhui Province have collapsed one after another, most of them are small dikes and newly built beaches. If there is no heavy rain in the next half month or a strong surge of water from the upper reaches, the large dikes along the river will not be in danger. According to the observation of an agricultural expert, the areas north and south of the Yangtze River in Anhui Province are fertile land with abundant grain production. Although many places are currently flooded, the damage is not great because it is temporary. If there is no heavy rain or flood, a bumper harvest is expected in the autumn. The seedlings in the counties and villages are growing day by day. It is expected that the new rice will be on the market by the end of this month. The provincial government, in order to intensify flood defense, recently sent telegrams to various counties along the river, providing some instructions. The main points are as follows: (1) In the event of flooding, all efforts should be made to defend against it. The orders have been issued to follow up on all cases with speed. How is the water situation in your county now? Are there any dangerous places? Please reply immediately, step up the defense, and do not be negligent or delayed. (2) Flood prevention is an urgent matter, and cooperation is essential to achieve success. In addition to the personnel of the Water Conservancy Engineering Committee and the Dike Works Committee, all district chiefs, baojia chiefs, and strongmen's teams must be fully mobilized to maximize effectiveness. Please comply immediately. (3) During the flood prevention period, dangers often occur unintentionally. Close patrols are paramount. The orders have been issued for compliance. It is sincerely feared that the dikes have not been fully noticed. Please quickly dispatch the responsible people to inspect the dikes step by step, day and night, and report them to the responsible personnel of the dikes, and repair and protect them according to law. For households living near the dikes, they should be ordered to find out if there are any leaks inside the house and build them strong at any time. (12th)

Guangzhou Suburbs Suffer Flooding: Mountain Torrents Arrive Suddenly Outside the Northeast and West Gates; Water Depth of Four to Five Feet, Houses Collapse and Injure People

Guangzhou Correspondence: The suburbs of Guangzhou have suffered flooding in recent years. Last year, the Old People's Home outside the East Gate was flooded, and dozens of old people drowned inside, resulting in an unprecedented tragedy in the city. After relief efforts from all parties and research on future flood prevention measures, it was agreed that the six-pulse canal, the Jade Belt River, and the East and West Moats in the old city of Guangzhou have been silted up for many years, and flood prevention will not be possible unless they are dredged. Because the city of Guangzhou is backed by the Baiyun and Yuexiu Mountains, mountain torrents pour into the suburbs after heavy rains. If the ring city canals and moats are unblocked, they can be used to discharge the mountain torrents, and the flooding of the city should not be too great. However, the dredging of canals and moats, although once proposed, was ultimately suspended due to doubts. As time passed, the situation changed, and until July 5th of this year, the suburbs suffered a second flood. On the afternoon of that day, the weather suddenly changed, and the sky was as dark as ink. At 6:00 PM in the evening, thunderstorms struck, like the Milky Way pouring down. The torrents from the Baiyun and Yuexiu Peaks surged to the northern suburbs. As a result, the streets of the Great North Gate, such as Jiulong Street, Lianhua Well, Rongshu Lane, Tiancao Temple, and Mangguoshu Street, were flooded in an instant, with the water depth reaching the shins. The houses on the streets were flooded to two or three feet. Qiantoutou outside the East Gate was more than four feet deep, and the Old People's Home became a lake. Fortunately, the person in charge of the home had moved the elderly to a safe place in advance. Outside the Old City Base outside the Little North Gate, the water was ten feet deep. Schools and restaurants in the suburbs were flooded. In addition, the water in Xiaobeilu, Fazheng Road, Xiaoshi Street, Dashi Street, and Haoxian Road was more than five feet deep. Six houses collapsed. The Xu residence at No. 10 Xiaobei Straight Street, the Huang residence at No. 19, the Wu residence at No. 20, the Xie residence at No. 27, the Zhu residence at No. 24, and the Zeng residence at No. 25 were all damaged. Five men and women were injured in the Zeng residence, one person was injured in the Zhu residence, two men and women were injured in the Huang residence, seven men and women were injured in the Wei residence, and three people were injured in the Wu residence. A total of 26 men and women were injured in the five residences. Outside the East Suburbs, in addition to the water depth reaching the navel in Qiantoutou, the nearby Shahe was also four feet deep. The floodwater on Shahe Road reached the knees. The area around the Yantang Military and Political School was seven feet deep. The Shahe Branch hired small boats to rescue the refugees. Many houses also collapsed on Shahe Main Street that night. Mountain torrents also flooded the Xicun area outside the West Suburbs. The ground of the provincial cement plant in Xicun was two feet high. The fire in the water tank was washed down and the fire in the furnace was extinguished. Work was temporarily suspended. By the morning of the 6th, the floodwaters had receded. The plant suffered a loss of several thousand yuan. (July 6th)

After the Yellow River Breach in Shandong: Han Sends Telegram Requesting Emergency Relief; Han Also Requests Disciplinary Action, Major Flood Has Passed Juancheng

Jinan Correspondence: Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, deeply knows that the dike breach this time in Juancheng will be difficult to plug up in a short period of time once the dike collapses. He is extremely guilty for the people affected by the disaster. At the same time, the personnel in charge of river affairs are responsible for their failure to protect against the breach. The original text is as follows: "Chengdu Committee Member Chiang, Nanjing National Government Chairman Lin, Executive Yuan President Han Junjian, National Economic Committee Chairman Song Ziwen Brother Xun Jian, Qie Huang Shui, Shandong Province, Juancheng County, Dongzhuang Linpu Collection, Dike embankment, I have already presented the overflow of various situations by Zhenri telegram, I want to invite Junjian, check the Yellow River breach in Dongming in the previous year, more than ten counties in western Shandong were submerged, the people suffered a great disaster, and their vitality has not yet recovered. Juancheng is now breached again, although I have supervised and ordered them to do their best to protect it, it is difficult to plug up the embankment. The people in the disaster areas in the previous ten or more counties will inevitably suffer another disaster. I am extremely guilty to hear the report. I presented it this spring and I was abused by the drought and the two wheat crops were poor. At present, the rain and ze have just been drenched, and I can be expected to have autumn. However, the late rice has not been planted yet, and I have suffered a deep cushion. My disaster victims, what should I do? I am wandering around the room, and my five internal organs are burning. I am responsible for comforting the people, and I cannot help but think of saving them. Only because the provincial treasury is exhausted, I am deeply ashamed of not being able to benefit from it. Xun orders the allocation of suspicious items and distributes them for tight relief to save the people's lives. I am responsible for my failure to supervise and inspect. In addition to ordering the chief and deputy chiefs to strictly investigate and take disciplinary action, please severely punish Fu Zuo and Director Zhang Lianjia of the River Affairs Bureau to warn and maintain law and discipline. At the time of the telegram, I was horrified to await orders. After the water situation, I will continue to telegram. My job is Han Fu Zuo Kou Zhenmi Shi Yin,"

The latest news received here on the evening of the 11th, combined with reports from long-distance calls from Juancheng and Yuncheng, stated that on the evening of the 10th, Juancheng was breached, and the water flowed in three streams. One was that the flood water exceeded the folk embankment and was sparsely flooded between Dongzhuang Linpu Jidong, and the flooded location was only more than 50 steps away from the Dongzhuang River Engineering Section. Several section workers were washed away by the flood and their whereabouts are unknown. The water was about 30 miles wide at the flood point, about 1 zhang high, and moved at a speed of 4 or 5 miles per hour. It passed Zheng Ying, south of Juancheng, on the afternoon of the 11th and arrived at Yinmaji, east of Juancheng, in the afternoon. The other two streams were caused by the breach of small folk embankments between Lishengtun and Yanglou. One stream flowed straight into Juancheng. Qin Daoyu, Magistrate of Juancheng County, led civilians and students from rural schools to block the breach with all their might, but the water was too strong and breached as it was being blocked. The water has reached Hongshankou between Juancheng and Juancheng, only 40 miles away from Yuncheng County. One stream flowed straight into Linpu Ji, and the water has reached the junction of Juancheng and Heze. The authorities are currently planning to guide the breached water into the Zhao Wang River, the Su River, and Nanwang Lake to prevent the disaster area from expanding. According to the telegram from Bai Daocun, Magistrate of Yuncheng County, on the 11th, the water flowing straight into Linpu Ji was about 8 feet deep and had reached the Li Gai area of Juancheng, with the water head being more than 2 feet high. The authorities are supervising civilians to help block the folk dike of Yinmaji in Juancheng, and also building a folk dike in sections for 50 miles from Maidougou in Yuncheng to Runshenkou to connect with the folk dike of Yinma Ji, so as to force the water from the breach into the Zhao Wang Su River and Nanwang Lake. (11th night)

Drowning Death from Falling into the River while Riding a Bicycle

Xia Tiesheng from Zhuanqiao, who runs the Xia Yuxing tea and food store, is doing well in business. His son, Guizhang, 22 years old, was riding a bicycle from Zhuan to Xinzhuang on the afternoon of the 13th. When passing the Zhu Dianshui Bridge south of Xin Zhuang Station, he accidentally fell into the river with the bicycle and drowned at that time. After receiving the report, Dong, a patrolman from the Sixth Branch Office of the Mountain, led the police to rush to the scene and found it to be true. The body and the bicycle were fished out and placed on the bank. Just as they were preparing to order the map and township police to report to the court for inspection, Guizhang's father arrived, recognized his son, and requested permission to waive the inspection and transport him back for coffin burial. A Prisoner Extortion Discovered and Interrogated

Zhang Ziming, a prisoner in the county prison, is from Tinglin and was sentenced to 20 years. Zhang Shuisheng, from Shanghai, was sentenced to 18 years. Both were involved in theft cases. Their appeals to the Shanghai High Court were rejected. They are arrogant and specialize in extorting new prisoners in prison. Previously, the court authorities remotely heard cries for help in the prison and went to investigate. Water Police Capture Robber Bandits on Boat

The First Brigade of the Zhejiang Water Police, acting on a confidential report that the ringleaders of the bandits who robbed the Shenhu-bound Jili steamboat at Zhangjiabang were hiding in Suzhou, dispatched Special Agent Hu Dongsheng to Suzhou on the 12th. Lin and Bai confessed to having collaborated with Gu and dozens of others in robbing the Jili steamboat without denying it. Mysterious Murder Case Still Under Investigation

The murder case in Guanning Lane is full of strange twists and has shocked society. In addition to the seven police officers, on the 12th, the Public Security Bureau transferred the case to the local court. At the time, the First Branch Bureau Chief Yan specially sent the newspaper with bloodstained fingerprints to the capital, requesting the fingerprint expert Xia Yinquan, head of the Beijing Police Department's detective team, to analyze the fingerprints in order to compare them with the fingerprints taken from the detained police officers, hoping to find the real culprit. It is reported that the Branch Bureau Chief returned to Suzhou at noon on the 13th. The result was that the bloodstains on the newspaper were more than sixteen hours old, and the blood was dry and shrunken, and the effectiveness of the analysis had been lost, so there was no concrete proof. The focus of the case has now shifted to the court, and the Public Security Bureau's investigation of the murderer has been unsuccessful.

Industry Association Cables Request for Publication of the Use of Silk Improvement Fees

The Wuxi Cocoon Industry and Silk Factory Associations are requesting clear publication of the exact amount and use of the improvement fees collected by the Jiangsu Construction Department for this year's spring cocoons, as they have not been announced. The original telegram is as follows: "Shen Junjian, Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, it is reported that the Jiangsu Province has established an Agricultural Management Committee, which has been approved by the Provincial Government Committee. The organizational regulations consist of ten articles, including Article 2, which defines the powers of the committee as (2) the guidance and improvement of the silk industry. The original Silk Industry Improvement Committee of Jiangsu Province, after the establishment of the Agricultural Management Committee, we deeply suspect, will the Silk Industry Improvement Committee still exist as before? The Silk Industry Improvement Management Committee has set up an office in Wuxi this year to supervise the collection of silk industry improvement fees, which is extremely diligent. The exact amount of improvement fees collected this spring has not been published. It is said that it is no less than 300,000 yuan. This improvement fee is entirely the lifeblood of silk and cocoon merchants. At a time when the rural economy is collapsing and the silk industry is in extreme decline, it is extremely difficult for silk and cocoon merchants to pay the improvement fee. It should be taken from the silk industry and used for the silk industry. Our association has repeatedly received inquiries from members about the exact amount collected this year and how it will be used. Therefore, we send a special telegram to report this matter, and respectfully request that the exact amount and use of the improvement fee collected this year be clearly announced to dispel public doubts and show great trust."

Yangzhou

Black Hen Lays Three-Yolked Giant Egg

Yang Fuzhi (History and Geography teacher at Aurora College), a resident of No. 13 Tangfang Lane, Quekou Street, Xincheng, Yangzhou, has a black hen, of an ordinary breed, but rather fat. It laid a double-yolked egg once last year, and on the morning of the 12th, it laid another egg, as large as a goose egg, weighing six taels on the old scale, or about seven taels on the new scale. The owner cut it open and found that it had three yolks. The reporter and Xi Jingyuan, a reporter from the Jiangsu Provincial Newspaper in Yangzhou, both witnessed the event and recorded this anomaly.

Local News

Confucius' Descendant, Kong Decheng, Arrives in Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday, Visits Various Construction Projects at the Invitation of Minister of Finance Kong, and Visits the Ancient Music Research Institute, Returning to Beijing Tonight

Confucius' descendant, Kong Decheng, arrived in Shanghai this morning at 7:01 AM via an overnight express train from Beijing, at the invitation of Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi to tour the city. Local municipal authorities dispatched staff to welcome him at the station. Upon disembarking, Kong proceeded directly to the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Finance on Rue West End to rest. He will visit various construction projects in the city and is scheduled to return to Beijing tonight on an overnight express train to attend the banquet at the Central Military Academy on the 15th, before returning to Shandong from Beijing. The details of his arrival in Shanghai are as follows:

Grand Welcome

Kong was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 12th, but was delayed until yesterday morning. Many representatives from Shanghai's municipal and other sectors gathered at the North Station to welcome him, including Li Qingxuan, Counselor of the Ministry of Finance and representative of Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, Chen Yi, Chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government, Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, Li Dachao, representative of Mayor Wu, Gan Hailan, Adjutant General of the Songhu Garrison Command, Wang Zhinan, representative of the Municipal Security Department, Wen Hongyin, Central Committee Member Wang Boqun and his wife, Zhang Renkui and Zhao Pinsan, representatives of the Shandong Association in Shanghai. The Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Security Department dispatched armed police teams to guard the North Station. The Shandong Association in Shanghai also hung banners at the station welcoming the Descendant of Confucius.

Kong's Demeanor

Kong is sixteen years old and a 77th-generation descendant of Confucius. This is his first time in Shanghai, and he was accompanied by his relatives Kong Yinqiu and Kong Xiangmian. Yan Shiyong, Zeng Fanshan, and Meng Qingtang, the three officials of the Confucius Temple, were originally scheduled to travel to Shanghai together, but urgently returned to their hometowns and departed from Beijing in advance. Kong was in good spirits, with a yellow-black complexion, wearing a blue silk gown, black leather shoes, and a straw hat. After getting off the train, he thanked the welcoming personnel at the station and was escorted to the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Finance on Rue West End to rest.

Statement

Upon arriving in Shanghai yesterday morning, Kong met with reporters in the reception room of the North Station and stated that he was deeply grateful for the warm welcome from all sectors in Beijing and Shanghai. He said that he came to Shanghai at the invitation of Minister of Finance Kong to visit various construction projects in the city and to pay respects to Mrs. Kong, and that he would also visit the newly established Ancient Music Research Institute on the sea for reference, as one is being planned in Shandong. He added that he would not stay in Shanghai for long and would return to Beijing on the overnight express train on the 14th, as the Central Military Academy had scheduled a banquet in Beijing on the 15th, which he had to attend. Kong said that this was his first visit to Beijing and Shanghai and that he had a very good impression of the south. Kong does not speak Mandarin, and his words were conveyed by his accompanying relatives.

Kong also issued a written statement yesterday, saying that Sun Yat-sen's advocacy of the Three Principles of the People and the idea that the world belongs to everyone, as well as Chiang Kai-shek's New Life Movement, are all good plans for saving China and revitalizing the nation, and that their origins are all from the teachings of the sages. He said that he most admired the government's respect for the sacred teachings, which allows the people's thoughts to have a center, the nation's organization to be united, and the national spirit to be restored. He also expressed his admiration for the rapid progress of construction in Nanjing, which was once a famous capital, in the few years since it became the capital, demonstrating the great strength of the national government.

Minister of Finance's Banquet

Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi is a 75th-generation descendant of Confucius, but his family moved from Shandong to Shanxi long ago and is a descendant of the descendant of Confucius. Therefore, he specially invited Kong to visit Shanghai in his own name. Minister Kong scheduled a banquet at his private residence last night, and the Descendant of Confucius was scheduled to visit Minister Kong and his wife at the Kong residence in the afternoon. They are also scheduled to visit various places today. According to Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, who welcomed Kong at the station, the Descendant of Confucius will go to Hangzhou to visit the scenic spots of the Three Temples and Six Bridges after arriving in Shanghai.

Kong Decheng, Descendant of Confucius (standing in the center), arriving in Shanghai (photo by Xu Tianzhang)

France's National Day Today, Officials and Nationals Celebrate Enthusiastically

Today is the 146th anniversary of France's National Day. The country's officials and nationals in Shanghai are holding grand celebrations as they do every year. The French Concession is decorated with lanterns and ribbons, officials are holding receptions, and government officials and the public are not working. The details are as follows:

Consul-General's Tea Party

The originally planned military parade by the Celebration Committee has been cancelled due to the hot weather. The celebration program began with a flag-raising ceremony at the French Consulate on Gongguan Road. From 11:30 AM to 12:30 PM, Acting French Consul-General Badas held a tea party at the consulate to receive congratulations from officials from various countries. Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of the city, Yu Ming, Director of the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and ambassadors and consuls from various countries in Shanghai will attend.

Official and National Gathering

Next, at 1:00 PM, members of the French General Association will have a luncheon at the clubhouse on Huanlong Road, and foreign guests will be invited. Senior police officers from the Public Concession were all invited. In addition, a children's carnival will be held at Gujiazhai Park at 4:00 PM. All French government, business, agencies and organizations will be closed today to celebrate.

Decorations

The Celebration Committee had been preparing everything for the celebration for the past month, and the preparations were completed yesterday. Starting yesterday morning, all shops, trams, and buses in the French Concession hung flags and ribbons. The electric torch arches erected on the Bund of the French Concession and the electric torches along Gongguan Road and Avenue Joffre were all lit up at 7:00 PM last night. The Celebration Committee has rated the lanterns and decorations hung by residents along the roads and awarded bonuses: 200 yuan for one first prize, 100 yuan each for two second prizes, and 50 yuan each for six third prizes. In addition, during the flag-raising ceremony in the morning, the French Concession authorities also awarded medals to officials of the Public Works Bureau and the patrol room.

Band Participation

The Shanghai Municipal Council Military Band usually performs at Zhaofeng Park from 10:00 AM to 11:30 AM every Sunday morning. However, today (the 14th) is France's National Day, and the Shanghai Municipal Council Band has been hired by the French Concession authorities to perform at the French Consulate General from 11:00 AM to 12:30 PM. Therefore, the original performance at Zhaofeng Park will be cancelled today.

Xu Shiying to Depart Tomorrow to Survey Disaster, Issues Written Statement

According to the Central News Agency, Xu Shiying, Chairman of the National Relief Commission, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing the night before last. He is scheduled to depart tomorrow night on the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiang'an ship to inspect the flood situation along the Yangtze River. According to Xu, he will travel along the Yangtze River from Jiangsu, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan to Changsha. Regarding the flood relief issue, he will temporarily allocate one million yuan from the disaster relief fund to meet immediate needs. Xu also issued a written statement as follows:

Rapid Rise

Before mid-June, various places suffered from drought, but after mid-June, continuous rain fell in the provinces along the river, and mountain floods occurred. The capacity of reservoirs and ponds in various places has been decreasing daily, resulting in insufficient discharge and rising water levels. According to reports from the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, except for Chongqing in the upper reaches, where the current water level is lower than the same period in the 20th year, the water level in all other places below Yichang is higher, and the rapid rise in the ten days since July 1 has been particularly alarming.

Reports of Disaster Pour In

The Relief Commission has repeatedly received letters and telegrams from Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui provinces reporting on the disaster situation. The severity of the situation is similar to the early stages of the floods in the 20th year. Fortunately, the Economic Commission, the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission, and the responsible agencies of the provincial and municipal governments, as well as local people, are making concerted efforts in flood prevention. President Wang, Chairman Chiang, and Vice President Kong, as well as Director Zhang of the Wuchang Provisional Headquarters, are also extremely concerned and are providing guidance at any time. Chiang has ordered precautions to be taken. The disasters have not yet fully expanded due to human intervention. However, it has been reported that 23 counties in Hunan, 12 counties in Hubei, 34 counties in Jiangxi, and Huaining and Qianshan counties in Anhui have been affected. In addition to the main stream of the Yangtze River, some areas of the Han River, Xiang River, Zi River, Yuan River, Feng River, Gan River, and Dongting and Poyang Lakes have also been flooded. Due to excessive rainfall and flash floods, 17 counties in Zhejiang Province have also reported disasters.

Departure for Inspection

Judging from the weather in recent days, the Beijing and Shanghai areas have been sunny every day, and the climate is quite normal. It may not rain in the next few days, but the water situation in the upper reaches is still worrying. On the 6th of this month, the Commission had already compiled a summary of the flood situation in various provinces and reported it to the Executive Yuan for review. At the same time, it sought detailed figures from various parties. Shi Ying himself is scheduled to travel by ship from Shanghai to the provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei to inspect the situation on the 15th of this month, and to discuss relief measures with the authorities in each province. At the same time, he will urge each province to include disaster relief funds in this year's budget, and establish a management committee to actively carry out the plan, so that there will be preparations and benefits for both the central and local governments.

Yellow River Also Rising

The water level of the Yellow River has also been rising sharply in recent days. According to reports, the county seat of Yanshi has been completely submerged. In addition, provinces such as Sichuan, Guizhou, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Fujian, and Zhejiang have also sent documents reporting heavy water and drought disasters. Due to time constraints, it is not possible to inspect everything this time. If necessary, more personnel will be sent in the future.

Changwang Vessels to Hold Agreement Meeting Tomorrow, Final Discussions on All Issues, Expected to be Implemented by the 22nd of This Month

In order to save the Yangtze River shipping line from price competition, the six major shipping companies in Shanghai, including China Merchants, San Bei, Ning Shao, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, and Nisshin, are planning to organize a freight pool agreement to maintain their interests. After several meetings, various measures have been drafted and finalized. A meeting is now scheduled to be held at 2:00 PM on the 15th to discuss everything. It is expected that the agreement can be implemented on the 22nd of this month. The details are as follows:

Meeting Tomorrow for Final Decision

The freight pool agreement organized by the six companies listed above was originally scheduled to be implemented on the 8th of this month, but has been repeatedly delayed for various reasons. Nisshin Steamship Company even requested an additional 15% discount, which led to a stalemate. Nisshin Steamship Company voluntarily canceled the request, and instead proposed to increase the number of voyages. According to Mr. Yamanaka, the manager of Nisshin Steamship Company, who spoke to a reporter from the Central News Agency yesterday, there was no such thing as a request for a 15% discount. All outside rumors are misunderstandings. The freight pool agreement is scheduled to be held at 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 15th. All issues will be discussed at that time, and a final decision will be made.

Realization is Expected, Trial Run for Six Months

According to sources, it is said that it will be implemented on the 16th of this month. There is not enough time. It will probably have to be extended for another week. Nisshin's Yamanaka also said that if there are no unexpected obstacles, the agreement is expected to be implemented on the 22nd of this month. In order to facilitate the procedures, each company has appointed specialists to form a temporary organization, named YanglzeRule, and has invited accountants Xi Wangshu and Thomson to calculate the accounts. A six-month trial period has been set.

Page 14

The Maiden Voyage of the "Mauli No. 2" Ended in Sinking at Dinghai Wharf Last Night; Incident Caused by Water Entering Through the Side Port Due to Crowds of Onlookers, Resulting in a Total Loss of Goods Worth 50,000 Yuan; Details of Whether There Were Drownings Are Unknown, But the General Bureau Dispatched Engineers and Others to Rush to the Scene Last Night for Salvage

The Mauli Commercial Steamship General Bureau's newly built "Mauli No. 2" steamship, which departed from Shanghai on its maiden voyage to Taizhou on the 11th of this month, sank at the Dinghai wharf last night (the 12th). The General Bureau has entrusted the China Salvage Company to dispatch engineers and workers, who boarded the Daxing steamship last night to rush to the scene to deal with the aftermath, where the goods, worth over 50,000 yuan, were completely lost. The details are as follows:

Maiden Voyage

The Mauli Steamship General Bureau, located at No. 4 Hengxin Lane, Wai Ma Road, Nanshi, Shanghai, operates the Mauli steamships on the Shanghai-Dinghai-Shipu-Haimen-Huangyan route. In order to develop the shipping industry and facilitate passenger and cargo transport between Shanghai and Taizhou, considering that the Mauli steamships were insufficient in both cabin space and tonnage, the Bureau specially ordered the "Mauli No. 2", a steel-hulled, double-bottomed express steamer, from overseas. After its construction was completed by the Sino-French Qiuxin Shipyard, it departed from Shanghai for its maiden voyage to Dinghai, Putuo, Shipu, Haimen, and Huangyan at 5:00 PM on the 11th of this month.

Welcome at Dinghai

The steamship has a gross tonnage of 1,134 tons, a net tonnage of 661 tons, a length of 19.5 zhang, a width of 3 zhang, and a speed of 12 nautical miles per hour. The shipowner is Xu Yousheng, and the comprador is Shi Cantang. It arrived at the Dinghai wharf and docked at 4:00 PM on the 12th. The Dinghai branch of the Mauli Bureau prepared a large number of firecrackers and held a grand welcome ceremony on the wharf. At the same time, people from all walks of life in the area were invited to board the ship for a tour, and the visitors were very crowded. Those on board heard the sound of firecrackers and rushed to the deck on the shore side to view the welcome on the wharf.

Ship Capsized and Sank

The "Mauli No. 2" steamship, due to uneven weight distribution, began to tilt towards the shore side by 7:00 PM. Visitors rushed to escape ashore, causing the ship to tilt even further. The shipowner, Xu Yousheng, and others tried their best to find a solution, but due to the large number of visitors, they could not persuade them to move. By 7:30 PM, the ship began to take on water through an open side port in the cabin, and it capsized and sank. A great chaos broke out, and the cries for help and weeping of those trying to escape filled the air. In about 20 minutes, the steamship sank next to the wharf.

Reported to Shanghai by Telegraph

The Shanghai General Bureau received a wireless report from the steamship at 6:00 PM on the 12th stating, "Ship arrived at Dinghai at 4:00 PM." At 9:00 PM, they received a telegram from the shipowner Xu Yousheng and others, "Ship capsized at Dinghai wharf, quickly devise a plan. Xu Yousheng, Hong Ashun, Song Linhua." At 9:16 PM, they received a telegram from the comprador Shi Cantang, "Ship sank alongside wharf, but not sideways. Three decks above the water level by two feet. Send divers to Dinghai for salvage. Crew member Miao (Shuizhang) accompanying [unclear] to handle the aftermath. Shi (Cantang)." At the same time, they also received a telegram from the Haimen branch, "Rumors of ship encountering danger in Dinghai, please confirm. What is the situation?"

Rushing to Salvage

After receiving the telegram, the General Bureau Manager Miao Shuizhang learned that the "Mauli No. 2" steamship had been insured with the China Ship Insurance Association for a sum of 90,000 yuan in national currency. In addition to notifying the Association, they entrusted the China Salvage Company to salvage the ship. The Company dispatched 32 engineers, workers, and divers, accompanied by Zhou Bolun from the General Bureau, who boarded the Lian'an Shipping Company's Daxing steamship from Shanghai at 5:00 PM yesterday afternoon and are expected to arrive in Dinghai this morning.

Total Loss of Goods

The steamship was carrying over 2,000 pieces of flour, over 6,000 pieces of soybean cake, 500 bags of rice, 70 pieces of hemp, and about 200 pieces of miscellaneous goods from the North and South, totaling about 370 tons, with a total value of about 50,000 yuan in national currency. The aforementioned goods were loaded by various businesses in Shipu, Haimen, Huangyan, and other ports. Since Dinghai was the first port on the Shanghai-Taizhou route, it was planned that after arriving in Dinghai, the ship would sail to Shipu, Haimen, and finally Huangyan. Therefore, the goods loaded were not unloaded. After the ship sank, all the loaded goods sank with it, resulting in a great loss.

Drowned Passengers

Regarding whether there were any drowned passengers or visitors who boarded the ship, the Shanghai General Bureau repeatedly received telegrams from the crew handling the matter, but none of them mentioned it. However, a telegram from Ningbo yesterday reported that a large number of passengers and visitors, about a hundred people, had drowned. Whether this is true cannot be confirmed at this time. However, according to an employee of the General Bureau, the sinking occurred by the wharf, and it was not a matter of a few minutes, so it is unlikely that anyone drowned. The detailed situation will be clear when the Lian'an Company's Zhoushan steamship arrives in Shanghai this morning.

Crew Members Return to Shanghai

Yesterday, many family members, relatives, and friends of the crew members and passengers who remained in Shanghai went to the General Bureau at No. 4 Hengxin Lane, Wai Ma Road, Nanshi, to inquire about the situation. The Bureau immediately replied with the telegrams from the shipowner and comprador. It is reported that the Lian'an Company's Zhoushan steamship has already载载了一部分船员返回上海, and is expected to arrive in Shanghai at 7:00 AM this morning and dock at the Guanqiao wharf in Nanshi. The sinking of the "Mauli No. 2" is truly a new record in the shipping industry.

Strict Investigation by the Central Relief Commission for the Issuance of Tax-Exempt Passports for Rice Relief

In past years, disaster areas in various provinces, facing food shortages, purchased rice from outside for relief. Each provincial government would request the Central Relief Commission to forward the request to the Ministry of Finance, which would then issue tax-exempt passports for purchasing rice. It is reported that the Commission conducts extremely thorough investigations of these passports. Last year, early rice crops suffered from disasters, resulting in severe conditions. The provinces of Zhejiang, Anhui, and Jiangsu all purchased foreign rice to relieve the disaster areas, and requested the issuance of tax-exempt passports. In order to ensure prudence and to understand the quantity of rice relieved and the various circumstances of purchase, transport, and relief distribution, the Relief Commission prepared an investigation form and distributed it to the original requesting agencies. Each item had to be filled out in detail and sent back for review. The investigation form is divided into eleven sections: (1) Original requesting agency, (2) Original quantity requested in shi, (3) Distributed disaster-stricken counties and quantity in shi (each shi equal to how many kilograms or market catties), (4) Receiving agency, (5) Person in charge, (6) Purchased from which port and which merchant, (7) Quantity reported to customs (each shi equal to how many kilograms or market catties), (8) Which merchant firm handled customs declaration, (9) Transported to where, (10) Date of departure, (11) Transported by train or boat. The provisions are extremely strict.

Then, Mr. Cheng gave his lecture, the main points of which are as follows: (1) The origin of economic panic, (2) International policies for dealing with economic panic, (3) The impact of economic panic on global labor unemployment, (4) Various methods for relieving unemployed workers.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Cables the Ministry of Finance Requesting Exemption from Transport and Sales Tax on Local Rice Wine

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, stating: "To the esteemed Ministry of Finance, Nanjing: On the 11th of this month, we received a letter from the Local Rice Wine Industry Association stating that, during the early years of the Republic of China, the local rice wine industry was at its peak, with over fifty workshops, each thriving. When the government levied a public sales tax in the fourth year of the Republic (1915), considering the special circumstances of the Shanghai region, where taxes were paid in the Chinese area but not in the foreign concessions, the Chinese area's commerce declined sharply. Commissioner Xie of the Second District Tobacco and Alcohol Affairs Bureau, recognizing the hardship, reported to the provincial bureau, which sent personnel to investigate and determine a special license, i.e., a half-tax certificate, for local rice wine in the Chinese area to be sold in the concessions. With this adjustment, the wine merchants managed to restore their businesses. For over a decade, tax revenues have increased rather than decreased. When the public sales tax was abolished and replaced with a fixed tax two years ago, it was expected that tax revenues would increase by one-quarter compared to the half-tax period. Contrary to expectations, revenues decreased by one-quarter. The reason is that, separated by a waterway, distilleries in the concessions can produce and sell wine without paying taxes, while distilleries in the Chinese area must pay eight jiao per hundred catties to sell wine in the concessions. Naturally, everyone seeks profit, so no one cares about selling wine from the Chinese area in the concessions. The number of workshops in the concessions has been increasing daily. Since the implementation of the fixed tax two years ago, more than half of the workshops in the Chinese area have closed down. If no measures are taken to relieve this situation, the future is precarious. It is undeniable that local rice wine is a subsidiary industry of farmers and is indeed a domestic product. Now that the government is actively promoting domestic products and has large-scale plans for various industries, either by raising loans or providing tax exemptions and incentives, why should our industry alone be left out? Now, our industry, recognizing that the Pubei China Alcohol Factory and the Zhabei Zhonghua Alcohol Factory, established by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and merchants, are temporarily exempted from taxes and have special stamps to show the difference when their products are sold in the Chinese area, these factories are flourishing. This approach is even better than the half-tax certificate treatment during the warlord era. Why is the current situation worse than before? The government's main goal is to promote domestic products. Our industry has the same domestic product nature and is located in the same special area. It seems that we can refer to the aforementioned approach, temporarily exempting taxes for sales within the special area to make adjustments and ensure fairness. Otherwise, our industry will be doomed. Statistics show that there are currently over twenty workshops, each employing between forty and fifty people, or twenty and thirty people, averaging close to a thousand workers. Counting their families, over ten thousand people rely on this for a living. If they are forced to close down, the suffering of displacement is unimaginable. Agriculture is the foundation of the country, and the foundation must be strong for the country to be secure. This is a teaching from the ancients. Our association pleads on behalf of the people and does not fear to repeatedly submit requests, offering our humble suggestions. We humbly request that your esteemed association forward this to the Ministries of Finance and Industry for approval, referring to the alcohol approach: local rice wine will pay taxes when sold within the Chinese area but be temporarily exempt from taxes when sold in the special area. When international negotiations are successfully concluded and the jurisdictional boundaries of the concessions are eliminated, so that all industries are treated equally and pay taxes, our industry will follow suit. This will at least allow Shanghai's local rice wine merchants to survive and not be completely wiped out. This is all thanks to the benevolence of the honorable officials. We are submitting this letter, requesting your esteemed association to review and forward it to ensure fairness and relieve the merchants' plight. These are the words that have reached the association. Upon investigation, it is found that foreign-owned alcohol factories within the concessions have not yet paid the unified tax, as evidenced by a Ministry of Finance approval. The case cited by the association, where the Pubei and Zhabei alcohol factories' products are temporarily allowed to be recorded as accounts when transported to the concessions, is because the concessions' alcohol has no tax, and this is the only way to compete. The situation with local rice wine is similar, as it is said that it is produced and sold within the concessions, but a fixed tax has not been levied. If it is allowed to develop freely, it will be difficult to manage. It is better to follow the example of inland alcohol factories recording accounts, and temporarily allow tax-free transportation for local rice wine transported from the Chinese area to the concessions. This will prevent the monopolization of profits, and it will be easier to negotiate a uniform tax in the future. This is truly a consideration for the national economy, not just for the self-interest of the wine merchants. Therefore, we are submitting this situation by telegram and requesting that your esteemed Ministry review and approve its implementation, for the sake of public convenience. [Signed] Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, respectfully."

The Rickshaw Industry Mutual Aid Association Held a Meeting Yesterday, Decided on the Date for Filing a Petition, and Notified all Rickshaw Owners to Hasten Their Registration

Since the Public Concession's Municipal Council decided to increase the rickshaw tax, the rickshaw owners have protested, believing they cannot bear the burden. They had previously requested the Chinese Ratepayers' Association to negotiate, but the Municipal Council has yet to respond. Yesterday, the industry's Mutual Aid Association held another meeting and decided on a date for filing a petition. Details are as follows:

Important Matters Decided

Those present at yesterday's meeting included Gao Youyu, Cheng Zhongdao, Ye Wenhua, Shen [unclear], and over twenty others. Ye Wenhua was elected chairman, and the agenda was as follows: 1. Report (omitted). 2. Registration among the industry has been very active in recent days (already exceeding 10,000 households). Due to the large number of people, there is concern that there may be radical actions outside that may violate the law and discipline. How should this be prevented? It was decided that (A) the Association will send personnel daily to investigate and guide at all times, and must abide by the Association's resolutions, wait quietly for negotiations to resolve the matter, and not take any action outside the guidelines; (B) the Association will issue a notice to persuade and advise. 3. The Municipal Council has not responded to the tax increase issue. How should we negotiate to urge an early resolution to reassure the industry? It was decided that (A) another letter will be sent to the Ratepayers' Association, requesting swift negotiations; (B) letters will be sent to all sectors and guilds, urging them to uphold fairness and provide assistance; (C) representatives will be elected to file a petition with the Chinese directors of the Municipal Council on a set date, requesting that they ask the Secretary-General of the Municipal Council, Zhong Si, to order the Vehicle Affairs Office to stop the tax increase.

Notice to Rickshaw Owners

This is clearly putting the rickshaw industry to death. We have now organized a Mutual Aid Association, as a whole group, to request the Chinese Ratepayers' Association and all sectors to provide assistance in requesting the Municipal Council to cancel the decision to increase the rickshaw tax, to preserve our livelihoods and reduce our suffering. This is currently in progress. We hope that all rickshaw owners will unite, peacefully conduct their business, and wait patiently for a resolution. Do not take any action outside the guidelines that may hinder the Association's work. This is to inform you."

The Municipal Council's Principle for Suppressing Inferior Alcohol is Limited to Those Harmful to Health, Counterfeit Brands Can be Resolved Through Law

The Shanghai Foreign Wine Association had previously submitted a request to the Municipal Council, stating that the market was flooded with inferior alcohol, hindering their business, and requesting the Council to suppress inferior alcohol in accordance with the methods of the French Concession authorities. They also requested that when applying for licenses, the contents of each bottle and the country of origin should be stated on the label. If the alcohol was imported in barrels and bottled in Shanghai, the bottler's name and address should be stated. If the alcohol was liquor, the alcohol content should also be stated. This matter has been repeatedly discussed in detail by the Public Concession's Defence Committee, together with the Police, Health, and Legal Departments. If the Municipal Council adopts the French Concession's method of suppressing inferior alcohol, would it conflict with the Public Concession's bylaws? Some say that if the nature of the alcohol is specified, alcohol standards must first be established. However, after they are established, how can inspections be carried out, and the procedures would be cumbersome. However, the new Chinese Criminal Code has now been implemented, and there are clear provisions for unscrupulous merchants who counterfeit brands and damage the credibility and interests of others. Therefore, the Municipal Council's Legal Department has the legal basis to file a lawsuit when such cases occur. Furthermore, if the Municipal Council approves the Foreign Wine Association's request and provides protection and assistance, how can it be handled without exceeding the scope of the Municipal Council's ordinary administration? All of the above points have been discussed in detail. According to the results of the Defence Committee's discussions, it was agreed that inferior alcohol should be suppressed, but only those harmful to health should be targeted. As for cases of counterfeit brands and sales of inferior alcohol, the wine merchants themselves have legal channels to resolve the matter. Therefore, the Association's request to add various restrictions when applying for licenses is clearly outside the scope of the Municipal Council's ordinary powers. Therefore, the request cannot be approved. It is heard that the Municipal Council's Board of Directors passed the Defence Committee's decision at a meeting the other day and sent a letter to the Association.

The Municipal Public Security Bureau Orders Its Subordinates to Strictly Prohibit Yin-Yang Calendars and Asks the Concession Police to Assist in the Investigation, Confiscation, Destruction and Punishment to Warn Cunning Scoundrels

Since our country implemented the Gregorian calendar, the lunar calendar has long been abolished. However, recently there have still been some unscrupulous merchants in the publishing industry who privately print these calendars for the sake of profit, misleading the public. Therefore, although there have been repeated orders and prohibitions, these [unclear] scoundrels have disobeyed in word but not in deed. Now it is again the time for printing. If they are not investigated and prohibited early, not only will the laws become waste paper, but unscrupulous merchants in the publishing industry will also be rampant. The corrupt and immoral lunar calendars will again appear on the market. The Municipal Public Security Bureau has been ordered to investigate and prohibit this. Director Cai specially issued an order to the various sub-bureaus and police stations under his jurisdiction yesterday to do so. The original order stated: "In accordance with the Municipal Government's Order No. 14601, 'In accordance with the presentation by Lu Jianqiu and others, regarding the private printing of Yin-Yang calendars in defiance of the National Government's explicit order, we request the reiteration of confiscation, destruction, and punishment to warn cunning scoundrels who are difficult to control. Continued News of Robbery on Wuzhen Road

At 6:45 PM on the 11th of this month, Liu Yuqing, a clerk from Hongchang Qianzhuang at No. 413 Sichuan Road, Nanjing Road, received account money, suspected of being silver dollars amounting to 7,000 yuan, in Zhabei. While riding in a chartered car southward via the Xin Zha Bridge, a group of robbers dragged Liu's car to a side road east of there, robbing him of 5,000 yuan in silver dollars near the entrance of Yongshou Lane. Two robbers fled towards Zhabei via Wuzhen Road and were subsequently apprehended by the Wuzhen Road police and others, along with a pistol. This was previously reported in the newspapers. It is now known that one of those apprehended by the Wuzhen Road police, Zou Shuigen, along with the victim Liu Yuqing and 1,000 yuan of the stolen money, were escorted to the Xin Zha Branch Bureau. According to Liu Yuqing, "I work as a runner for Hongchang, collecting accounts in Zhabei every day. Unexpectedly, this time I was targeted by robbers who snatched 5,000 yuan in silver dollars south of the Xin Zha Bridge. Three people were involved, and after the robbery, they fled into Yongshou Lane, escaping through the south alley." The rest of his statement was similar to the newspaper report. Zou Shuigen, however, claimed, "I was actually coming out of a friend's house, thinking of going to cool off on the Wuzhen Road bridge. Suddenly, I heard gunshots. Since I am new to Shanghai, I didn't understand the situation, so I followed them and ran. Unexpectedly, I was hit by two bullets, one in my right shoulder and one in my waist. Both were only superficial wounds. Who knew the police would arrest me and treat me like a robber? It's a real injustice!" After examining the confessions, the examining magistrate, noting that the case involved Police Chief Hu Yao and officers such as Hu Kui of this branch bureau pursuing the robbers to the jurisdiction of the Mongol Road Police Station and capturing them, and that the victim had identified them and a pistol was found, saw no reason to doubt the account. He therefore ordered that Zou Shuigen and the 1,000 yuan in silver dollars be transferred to the Public Security Bureau. Although Detective Weng Peiyu of the Public Concession and Western Detective Chief Bao Dai requested that the robbers be brought back to the Concession, the examining magistrate refused, stating that the robbers dared to fire shots along the way, resisting arrest and injuring officers and pedestrians. He instructed them to request extradition from the Public Security Bureau. It is also known that Yu Chuntao, who was also apprehended in this case, was escorted to the Public Security Bureau by the Mongol Road Police Station on the preceding two days. As for the injured police officer, Li Chao Kui, a bullet entered the instep of his foot, and his leather shoe was also pierced. A pedestrian named Wu Qiyao was struck by a stray bullet in the leg. Yesterday, Inspector Luo Siwei of the Wuzhen Road Police Station visited them at Baojiang Hospital and the Chinese Red Cross, respectively. The injuries of the injured individuals were not critical, so there was no danger to their lives, and they would be able to be discharged in a few days.

Zhao Xiaomei, a young girl from Taizhou, aged fifteen, made a living by selling apples. Yesterday morning at seven o'clock, she carried a basket of apples to the Putong Huatong Wharf to sell them. Murder Case of Watchman: Shen Lianfa Autopsied; Deceased's Pistol Bullets Untouched; Source of Assailant's Finger Injury Unknown

Shen Lianfa, a 35-year-old Shandong native and watchman at Qingcheng Qianzhuang, No. 1589 Fushui Lane, Tianjin Road, had a verbal dispute with Wang Dongchun, a 41-year-old Haizhou native and gate watchman at No. 35 of the same lane, the night before last at around 10 PM. Wang suddenly drew a pistol and fired four shots at Shen, hitting him in the head and legs twice, causing serious injuries. Wang sustained only a slight injury to his right finger. Officers No. 1264 and No. 477 from the General Police Station responded to the scene and apprehended Wang, taking him to the police station. Shen was taken by ambulance to Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died shortly after. The body was taken to the coroner's office on Ferron Road. Detective Chief Wu Yaozu and detectives Zhu Wanjun, along with Western detectives, went to the scene to investigate. Yesterday morning, the murderer Wang Dongchun was sent to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division One. The police station's lawyer, Ru Baoquan, presented the case and filed a public prosecution under Article 371, Paragraph 1 of the New Criminal Code, requesting an extension for further detailed investigation. Wang Dongchun confessed that he was a gate watchman residing at No. 392 Dongyouheng Road. The deceased had brought six women to an empty house in the lane on the evening of the 11th of this month for entertainment, which was seen by Sun Zhaosheng, another watchman, who expelled them all. The deceased suspected Wang of having instigated this, so he accosted him last night, leading to a dispute. Wang claimed that the deceased fired at him first, and he returned fire in self-defense. Realizing the gravity of the situation, he surrendered to the police. Witness Bai Ganting and others also provided statements. Judge Qian Hongye adjourned the hearing for one week for further questioning. Around 10 AM, Prosecutor Song Genshan from the court's prosecutor's office, along with forensic doctors Wei and Zhang and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the coroner's office to examine the body. According to Western Police Chief Shi Diwen's report on the investigation, the deceased's pistol was found at the scene by the police, still in its holster, and the five bullets issued to him were untouched. Therefore, the source of the murderer's finger injury is unknown. The deceased's family members are all in their hometown, and his friends have come to claim the body. After questioning Wang Dongchun briefly, Prosecutor Song determined that the deceased Shen Lianfa, male, died from gunshot wounds sustained during his lifetime. Wang Dongchun had already been investigated by the police. The body was allowed to be claimed by his friend Ma Zaiduan after he signed a guarantee.

Couple Commits Suicide by Poison in a Northern China Apartment, Leaving Behind a Child

At 10 PM on the 11th, a couple claiming to be Wang Ennian, 30 years old, and his wife Feng Qiuxin, 23 years old, from Suzhou, checked into Room 15 of the Northern China Apartment at No. 431 Ximen Road, Malong Road in the French Concession with a child. The bellboy led them to the room, which cost seven silver dollars per night. On the evening of the 12th, they stayed for another night. At 0:30 PM yesterday, Wang and his wife had not gotten up, and the child was crying incessantly. The bellboy, Shang Xiufeng (30 years old, from Hebei), knocked on the door, but there was no response for a long time. Suspecting something was wrong, he tried to open the door, but it was bolted from the inside. He looked through the window and saw the man dead on the bed and the woman barely breathing. Greatly alarmed, he informed the cashier and reported to the French police, who dispatched detectives to investigate. Two empty opium boxes were found, confirming that they had committed suicide by poison. Two suicide notes were also found. The woman and child were taken to Guangci Hospital for treatment, while the man's body was taken to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for autopsy. The woman succumbed to the poison shortly after arriving at Guangci Hospital. The child was temporarily left at the hospital, and the woman's body was also sent to the coroner's office to await examination by officials from the Second Special Court tomorrow. Detectives are investigating the families of the deceased.

Song Xueqin Admits Li Zhen Is His Daughter; Bo Zhen Says Lawsuit Is Unnecessary; Judge Orders Song to Appear in Court for Reconciliation

Song Xueqin, the director of the Shanghai office of Sun Chuanfang, the former commander of the Five-Province Allied Forces, married Bo Xuezhen, a woman from Wuxian, as his concubine in 1921. They lived in Hankou and had a daughter in 1925, named Li Zhen, who is now eleven years old. At that time, their relationship was quite good. However, in May 1931, Song began living with a prostitute surnamed Zhu, and the loving relationship of more than ten years came to an end. They divorced, and Song gave Bo 20,000 yuan for living expenses, with a signed separation agreement stating that Li Zhen would be raised by Bo. Recently, Bo felt that Song was ignoring Li Zhen altogether, and fearing future disputes, she hired lawyers Zhang Shizhao, Xiang Xun, and Peng Yuanxun to file a lawsuit in the First Special Court to confirm the daughter's parentage. The case had been heard once before. Yesterday morning, Judge Peng Yishi opened the Fourth Civil Division to hear the case. Song Xueqin did not appear, and his lawyer stated that Song had gone to Beiping for important matters and could not arrive today. Bo Xuezhen first stated the circumstances of the case. The defendant's lawyer argued that of the 20,000 yuan given at the time of the separation, 10,000 yuan was for Li Zhen's education and other expenses. Song is currently distributing his assets, with each of his four sons receiving 20,000 yuan and each of his four daughters receiving 10,000 yuan. Therefore, Song has not denied that Li Zhen is his daughter, and the plaintiff's lawsuit is unnecessary. Judge Peng also noted that the separation agreement stated the words "daughter Li Zhen," so her identity was already established, and there was no need for further litigation. The plaintiff's lawyer then stated that the purpose of the lawsuit was not to seek anything, but to prevent disputes over inheritance after Song's death, so they filed the lawsuit. Now that the defendant does not deny paternity, they requested that the court order Song to appear in court to make a settlement record, so that Li Zhen could be recognized. The court, considering that this was a personal lawsuit, could order Song to appear in court for reconciliation. The hearing was adjourned to August 8, and Song was ordered to appear in court in person next time.
