Two Watermelon Vendors "Drinking Tea" [Mediation]; Police Interference Leads to Assault; Huang Chunfa Sentenced to Ten Days of Detention

Huang Chunfa, a 23-year-old native of Huzhou, is a fruit vendor. Recently, due to the hot weather, he set up a watermelon stand at the entrance of the Xixin Bridge vegetable market in the French Concession. A local named Ah Jin, who already had a watermelon stand there, saw that Huang's stand was stealing his business and stopped him from setting up his stand. Huang refused to yield and would not move, leading to a verbal dispute. Ah Jin invited Huang to "drink tea" [mediate] at the Xiafei Teahouse at the intersection of Xiafei Road and Glock Road on the morning of the 11th to resolve the matter. At the appointed time, both sides brought a large number of people, each holding wooden sticks and other weapons. Upon meeting, the two sides began fighting without asking any questions, attacking each other. While the two sides were engaged in a fierce brawl, officer No. 379, Wang Jia Yu (24 years old, from Jiangsu) of the French police station, heard the alarm on Minteyni Ying Road and rushed to the scene. At the entrance of Gui'an Lane on Glock Road, the two sides surrounded the police officer, intending to make trouble for him, and struck his shoulders with wooden sticks, tearing his uniform on the back. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the officer, realizing that he was outnumbered, fired a shot into the air and blew his whistle. Upon hearing the gunshot and whistle, the thugs scattered and fled. Officers from nearby stations rushed to the scene and helped to apprehend Huang Chunfa, seizing three wooden sticks used in the assault. He was taken to the police station and yesterday, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. Judge Dong Qiming interrogated him, and the Legal Affairs Department's lawyer, Gu Shouxi, presented the case, prosecuting him for obstructing official duties and insulting an officer. Officer No. 379 testified about the incident. After the court questioned the defendant, it sentenced Huang Chunfa in court to ten days of detention as a warning for assaulting and insulting a public official while he was performing his duties.

The Commercial Press Establishes a New Physics and Chemistry Laboratory; Divided into Paper, Chemical, and Instrument Sections; Paper Testing Equipment Is Particularly Comprehensive

The Commercial Press in this city, in order to standardize its products and supplies by identifying goods, establishing standards, researching manufacturing, and exploring scientific principles, established a physics and chemistry laboratory at its original site on Baoshan Road in Zhabei last year. It has now been established and hired Mr. Tang Lingge, a former researcher at the National Central Research Institute, to be in charge. The laboratory is divided into three sections: paper testing, chemical testing, and physical instrument and biological specimen testing, occupying approximately 5,000 square feet. The chemical section is equipped with ordinary instruments, as well as a refractometer, vacuum pump, ion titrator, electric centrifuge, viscometer, nitrogen determinator, constant-temperature electric oven, platinum ware, etc., which is sufficient to handle various chemical tests and research work. The paper testing laboratory has a photoelectric opacimeter, glarimeter, tensile strength tester, folding endurance tester, bursting strength tester, quadrant paper scale, thickness gauge, paper expansion and shrinkage tester, viscosity tester, hygrometer, fadometer, tearing tester, and indoor humidity controller, making it the most comprehensive paper testing laboratory in the country. It is said that the company needs this research because it uses many types of printing paper each year, in large quantities. In addition, the physical instrument and biological specimen testing laboratory is also equipped with precision instruments for testing. The above-mentioned instruments were directly ordered from scientific instrument manufacturing companies in Germany, England, and the United States, and are of considerable value. Most of the instruments have been installed and are starting to work.

Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company to Add Regular Special Buses to Shanghai-Dachang Line, Reducing Fares; Addition of Special Buses to Benefit Travelers Starting on the 16th

The Shanghai-Taicang Long-Distance Bus Company, a commercial enterprise in this city, in order to develop its business and facilitate travel for passengers, has decided to reduce fares on the Shanghai-Liuhang and Shanghai-Jiading lines and add special buses and Shanghai-Dachang special buses, starting on the 16th of this month, to benefit travelers. The details are as follows:

Implementation Announcement

The company's board of directors, in response to passengers' requests, decided at its board meeting on the 10th of this month to reduce fares on the Shanghai-Liuhang and Shanghai-Jiading lines and add special buses. Yesterday, it issued an announcement stating: "To whom it may concern, the current Shanghai-Liuhang and Shanghai-Jiading line fares need to be adjusted. The board of directors has approved the reduction of fares and the addition of special buses between Shanghai and Dachang. The special Shanghai-Dachang bus fares will also be reduced. All will be implemented starting on July 16. At the same time, the previous round-trip ticket and coupon system will be abolished. For detailed fare tables, please obtain them from the various stations. Also, the last bus from Shanghai Station every Saturday will be extended to depart at 5:45 PM. A special bus will be added from Jiading Station on Mondays at 7:30 AM. Please take note."

Fare Reduction

The original fare was calculated at 3.6 cents per kilometer. Now, the fare has been reduced to 3 cents per kilometer. The revised Shanghai-Liuhang line fares are as follows: Shanghai to Yuqing Bridge 18 cents, Dachang 21 cents, Tang Bridge 36 cents, Gujia Town 40 cents, Liuhang 49 cents, Changdan Bridge 59 cents, Luodian 69 cents, Panjia Bridge 84 cents, Shuangcaodun 97 cents, Shugou Bridge 1.01 yuan, and Liuhang River 1.11 yuan. For the Shanghai-Jiading line, from Shanghai to Luodian, and from Luodian to Jiading on the Shanghai-Liuhang line, the company, in response to requests from passengers and the Jiading County Construction Bureau, will reduce the fare completely. However, this preferential treatment is only available for passengers traveling from Shanghai to Jiading. The company has installed a sound system that reports the newly revised fares once or twice a day.

Addition of Special Buses

According to Zhu Gusheng, the director of the company's transportation department, the company used to run buses every two hours, departing from Jiading and Liuhang simultaneously. Finding that the time interval was too long, the company changed the schedule to alternate between the two lines. Now, in response to passengers' requests, it has been decided that, starting on the 16th of this month, the last bus departing from Shanghai every Saturday will be extended to depart at 5:45 PM. One special bus will be added from Jiading and Luodian each Monday. The bus from Jiading to Shanghai will depart at 7:30 AM, and the bus from Luodian to Shanghai will depart at 6:45 AM.

Shanghai-Dachang Special Buses

The original fare for the Shanghai-Dachang route was 26 cents, which has now been reduced to 18 cents. The fare from Shanghai to Yuqing Bridge is 13 cents, and from Yuqing Bridge to Dachang is 5 cents. A total of eleven special buses will be added every 30 minutes. The first bus from Shanghai will depart at 7:30 AM, and the last bus will depart at 5:30 PM. The first bus from Dachang will depart at 7:00 AM, and the last bus will depart at 5:00 PM. The fare is calculated at 2.6 cents per kilometer.

French Concession Rickshaw License Fee Payers Unanimously Oppose Registration of Rickshaw Pullers

Since the French Concession Public Works Bureau issued a notice that registration of public rickshaw pullers would begin on the 4th of this month, and that all registration request forms were stipulated to be three copies per vehicle, and that batches would be handed over to license fee payers for each vehicle owner and puller to comply with, to date, ten days, 3,300 copies of these registration request forms have been issued. Each vehicle owner can only painstakingly advise rickshaw pullers to register. Each rickshaw puller would rather abandon the vehicle than register, resulting in the registration office of the Public Works Bureau being deserted. Yesterday, each rickshaw license fee payer specifically jointly requested the Public Works Bureau to withdraw the order. The original text is recorded as follows: "Presented as a joint request to stop the registration of rickshaw pullers in order to maintain the rickshaw industry and show compassion for the coolies. It has been found that when your bureau dispatched personnel to investigate the real owners of rickshaws in the South Shanghai area this spring, rumors of rickshaw registration arose, causing panic among rickshaw pullers, who left Shanghai one after another. To this day, there is a shortage of rickshaw pullers in each rickshaw company, vehicles have stopped operating, and the situation has not yet returned to normal. We are seeking relief. Suddenly, we read in the newspaper that the police department of your bureau intends to implement rickshaw puller registration from the 4th of this month, and to add thumbprint fingerprints, etc. We specially urged each vehicle owner to comply, but each vehicle owner unanimously stated that although vehicle owners and rickshaw pullers are in close proximity, the rickshaw pullers have deeply entrenched views, and would rather beg for food than register, which is almost a universal sentiment. Once rickshaw pullers are forced to register, they will inevitably abandon the vehicle and leave, directly affecting the livelihoods of the poor and indirectly hindering the business of vehicle merchants. In any case, unless rickshaw pullers voluntarily register, vehicle merchants really have no way to imagine it. Furthermore, since your bureau stipulated a quota for annual license fee payment for the South Shanghai rickshaw industry, merchants have repeatedly requested improvement and relief from the public association for various losses such as paying for new licenses, returning old licenses, and rickshaw licenses being stolen, but have not been approved. On the rickshaw puller side, they operate all day, are indiscriminately photographed by the police, brave wind, rain, cold, and heat, and try to redeem their licenses. They are already extremely miserable waiting in front of various police stations. Sometimes the redeemed license is not the one photographed, or they have a good small ticket but cannot redeem it, and when the police station finds out, they fine the rickshaw puller double the amount. Thus, ignoring the hardships of rickshaw pullers on weekdays has already made rickshaw pullers regard the police station as a long journey. This time, the registration is out of benevolence and good governance, but how can rickshaw pullers not believe it? If it is forcibly implemented, no rickshaw puller will not be frightened and run away. These are all real situations, which can be verified immediately. Merchants will certainly comply with the intentions of your bureau, but with regard to the aspects of powerlessness and inability to comply, we now jointly request that your bureau consider the hardships of merchants and carefully consider the rickshaw puller registration method, and immediately stop the process, so as to avoid causing misunderstandings and unexpected losses. The merchants are fortunate, and so is society. We respectfully present this matter to the Director-General of the French Concession Public Works Bureau, jointly presented by the rickshaw license fee payers of the French Concession: Xia Xizheng, He Qipeng, Hu Wenqing, Cui Guangyu, Zhu Jinrong, Song Fengming, Shao Wenlong, Li Pingyu, He Jinxiang, Ju Ganxin, Zhu Wansheng, Yuan Changbao, Zhu Shihuan, Xue Zengfu, Zhou Jinting, Cai Jinshan, Qiu Chunshan, Zhang Huaiyang, Song Yaokun, Yu Dajin, Zhu Zhishan, Zhou Jinyuan, Liu Huanzhang, Zhao Tianyuan, Wang Rongqing, Wang Xueliu, Yuan Dehua, and more than 230 others."

Settlement of the Case of Public Bus Employees in Zhabei Beaten by Three Westerners

On the 21st of last month, at approximately 7:00 PM, Public Bus No. 4936 of the Shanghai Huashang Public Bus Company was returning from the Municipal Government to the North Station when it arrived near the Kailin Paint Company on Xitiyu Road. In order to avoid pedestrians in front of the bus, the driver quickly braked and stopped the bus. At the same time, three Westerners were approaching in a private car with license number 1430 issued by the Municipal Council. They also stopped the car, which angered them. They actually beat the bus driver, Gao Sanhou, and the ticket seller, Pan Linyun, causing serious injuries. The company saw that two employees were beaten for no reason and that the bus's travel time was delayed. They sent a letter to the Public Utility Bureau and the North Station Branch Bureau to investigate the perpetrators. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. (It is said that the Public Utility Bureau approved Xing and detained the car license of the Western perpetrators.) Therefore, on the 11th of this month, the Westerners sent representatives to the general manager of the Public Bus Company to resolve the matter peacefully. However, the company believed that the perpetrators had fled, violating criminal law, and that the case had been submitted to the authorities for handling. It was inconvenient to advocate for private reconciliation. The company consulted with the representatives at the North Station Branch Bureau to seek opinions before proceeding with the resolution. It was found that the material losses of the two injuries, such as medical expenses and wages lost due to injury, were fully compensated. As for the mental losses caused by the injury, the representatives and the Sixth District Public Bus Industry Union will resolve it separately.

The Chinese Amateur Wireless Society Appeals to the Government

The Chinese Amateur Wireless Society is the only wireless research organization in the country that connects comrades from all over the country with amateur wireless society members from various countries to conduct practical wireless experiments. Recently, in view of the fact that our country's wireless laws and amateur research regulations have not yet been promulgated, the society has submitted a document to the Ministry of Transportation for registration and requested the promulgation of wireless amateur research regulations. On the 8th of this month, the president, Fang Ziwei, and the vice president, Zhang Rangzhi, met with the Minister of Transportation, Zhu Jialin, to explain everything. Minister Zhu promised to approve it immediately. At the same time, a document was submitted to the Ministry of Education for record. Now that the Ministry of Transportation is secretly reporting private radio stations, the society has presented various advantages and disadvantages in the document to the Ministry of Transportation, and that amateur wireless should be encouraged and maintained by the government. It is very sincere. At the same time, it published advertisements in the newspaper (Shen Bao) for three days to summon amateur research comrades across the country to work together and petition the government authorities so that amateur benefits can be guaranteed and developed. Recently, the society has received responses from comrades across the country, and letters of support have been pouring in. The society was established after the September 18th Incident. Although it has only been four years, the society has spared no effort in its work, compiling and publishing the QSP Wireless Magazine every month, promoting academics, and achieving remarkable results. More than 200 comrades from all over the country have joined the society as members. The current president and vice president are Fang Ziwei and Zhang Rangzhi, both pioneers in amateur wireless research. This time, the two men led all the remaining people to work hard to appeal to the government authorities. It is expected that the future of our "Chinese Amateur Wireless" will be able to shine a ray of dawn.

The Beiqiao Town Organizes a Fire Brigade

The fire-fighting equipment in Beiqiao Town, Shanghai County, is still lacking. Yesterday afternoon, the district chief, Wang Cheng, and the director of the district farmers' association, Yang Zhuoyun, specially invited local people Zheng Guozhai, Cai Mengliang, Shi Ben, Cai Xiaoliang, Zhou Jinyuan, Zhang Shushan, etc., to gather at the district office to discuss the organization of the Beiqiao Fire Brigade. Each initiator determined the donation amount, and the remaining shortfall will be raised from the outside world. It was already sunset when the meeting adjourned. The fund-raising notice is also recorded as follows: "Fire protection is a national police facility, and fire-fighting is a local autonomous undertaking. Indeed, a spark of fire, if large, is related to the public's peace, and if small, is related to the life of the whole family. This is inherently impermanent and unpredictable. Don't you see the fire at the Xiajiazhai house in Xing? Connected buildings were reduced to ashes in an instant. Scorched heads and burnt faces are hard to approach in a moment. Brewing a catastrophe in the countryside is something that a cup of water cannot stop. Learning from past events is a lesson for the future. Therefore, prevention must be strict, and preparation must be early. This is why each neighboring district has organized a fire brigade. Since Beiqiao was built by the county government, there have been numerous institutions, connected houses, and an increasing population. There is no fire protection equipment. Even if we move the firewood away from the fire and bend the chimney, there may be one omission in a hundred precautions. A spark can start a fire, and preparedness can prevent trouble. When Magistrate Pan took office, he repeatedly said this (see the minutes of the 19th District Affairs Meeting on March 25, 23rd year). After we heard the order, we were at a loss. Time flies by, and a year has passed without any unexpected disasters. We should not avoid the pursuit of perfection. Now, we are fortunate to be led by the , who has allocated a large sum of money for planning again. It is a small supplement. Although it is said that horses and dragons are bustling, it is not necessarily possible to achieve our ambitions. However, empty hands and fists can at least be better than nothing. Therefore, we are going door to door to beg, imitating the cry of a burdened man, and collecting bits and pieces to form a robe, hoping that gentlemen will help us achieve our goals. It is related to our hometown, so we do not refuse anything, large or small. It is a contribution to the country, and praise and honor await. This is a notice jointly issued by the initiators Cai Yimengliang, Yang Zhuoyun, Zhang Shushan, etc."

The Trucking Industry Requests Exemption from Third-Party Liability Insurance and Sends a Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Asking Them to Forward It to Argue Their Case

The Trucking Industry Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, saying, "We, the undersigned, would like to report that since the increase of the 2.5% vehicle tax last year, we have also been ordered to uniformly purchase third-party liability insurance when renewing vehicle licenses starting in the winter of the 23rd year. We have previously submitted a request to the Public Utility Bureau, stating the difficulties faced by the industry and requesting that the practice of renting out taxis be followed, with both the purchase of third-party liability insurance and the payment of a security deposit being implemented simultaneously to show fairness. However, on October 8th of the same year, we received a reply that our request was not approved. Furthermore, we have received a joint letter from dozens of vehicle companies such as Yuan Zhiji Fuxing Tongxing, stating that since the increase of the 2.5% vehicle tax, they are already unable to bear the burden. However, because it concerns government tax revenue, they have no choice but to try their best to comply. Now, after increasing the vehicle tax, we are forcing all of our fellow industries in the city to uniformly purchase third-party liability insurance (all vehicles must submit an insurance policy and insurance receipt when renewing their license). Otherwise, even if the vehicle tax is paid, the license will not be renewed. If this is the case, then each vehicle of our entire industry must, in addition to paying a vehicle tax of approximately 200 yuan per quarter, also raise an insurance fee that is double the amount of the vehicle tax (approximately 200 yuan) in order to renew the license. In this time of economic depression and extreme scarcity of passengers and goods, the income from fares of our companies is not enough to cover expenses. The income from a day of hard work is not enough to maintain the livelihoods of our employees. Therefore, companies have a tendency to be unsure of what the next day will bring. The misery of their situation cannot be described in words. Therefore, we are forced to send a letter to your chamber, requesting that you forward it to the municipal authorities and request that the relevant department cancel this mandatory insurance measure.' Based on this, the municipal authorities ordered trucking companies to uniformly purchase third-party liability insurance, and its intention was originally excellent. However, in this economic downturn, merchants and industries are struggling to survive, and the decline of the trucking industry is particularly obvious. According to the latest statistics from the affiliated association, the number of trucks in this city has decreased by 30%. At this critical moment, forcing them to bear this mandatory insurance fee, which is double the amount of the vehicle tax, is tantamount to driving our entire industry to ruin. The affiliated association has silently observed the overall trend of the industry and deeply knows that the burden of this insurance fee is beyond the ability of the industry to bear. Currently, insurance is like business, and freedom should be the principle. If forced insurance is imposed, it seems unfair in terms of law, reason, and human sentiment. Your chamber leads various industries and is currently working hard to revitalize industry and commerce. We should ask you to follow the principle of relief and argue reasonably to allow you to forward this matter to the municipal government and inform the competent authorities, earnestly requesting that they revoke this regulation that requires third-party liability insurance to be purchased before a license can be issued, in order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants and provide relief. We are deeply grateful. Addressed to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce."

Using His Wife to Carry Drugs

Chen Jinsheng and Li Yinmin, Chinese detectives from the Sixing Road Police Station, learned that there was a small drug-selling organization that specialized in using women to carry drugs to various places for profit. At approximately 7:00 PM the night before last, they were waiting near Oujia Road and Tangen Road. After waiting for a while, they saw two locals, Zhang Wangshi and Sun Bingsheng from Pudong, walking leisurely and talking and laughing. Zhang was holding a package. The detectives stepped forward to stop them and opened the package, finding 78 taels of a substance that looked like white sugar. There was nothing else. They ordered Zhang to quickly hand over the drugs. Knowing that she could not escape the law, she took out one tael of morphine and 200 red pills from her side, saying that the contraband was brought to Pudong by a fleeing man named Chen, who promised to pay her two yuan as a reward. Sun was searched, and no drugs were found on him. The two were arrested and taken to the police station along with the evidence, where they were detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Gongbu Bureau, described the previous situation in detail and requested an extension to investigate and arrest the principal offender. Chen and Li then reported the process. The evidence was presented for inspection and questioned by the two defendants, whose statements were evasive. Judge Wu ordered that they be returned to detention separately for further verification at a later date.

Han Genfu Rescued After Attempting Suicide

Han Genfu, a 30-year-old Ningbo native, lived at No. 591, Kunming Road, Tangshan Road, Hongkou. At the end of December last year, he was arrested for opening a swallow's nest for people to smoke opium and sentenced to seven months in prison. He was only released on the 7th of this month. After returning home, he saw that his wife, Lin, was quite cold to him and that she was several months pregnant. He became suspicious and they quarreled with each other. Lin tried her best to defend herself, but to no avail. They agreed to commit suicide together by jumping into the river. At about 10:00 AM yesterday, they went to the outside of the Taikoo Wharf in the French Concession. Han first jumped into the river, but Lin suddenly realized that suicide was not the best way to prove her innocence, so she did not follow him. Han was soon rescued by Ding Jigui, a boatman from No. 626, and sent to the Customs Water Police Station. After questioning him about the details, he was also criticized for his mistake of taking his own life. Police officer Wang Haiquan was sent to bring his wife, Lin Xiaoyue, to take her husband back.

Inspection Report of the China Reclamation Bank

The China Reclamation Bank issued a report on the inspection of the issuance reserve, stating that the issuance treasury and the business treasury of the China Reclamation Bank have always been completely separated. On the 13th of this month, accountant Wang Zikang, together with Xu Jiqun and Xu Busun, representatives of the board of directors and supervisors, conducted an inspection, and the results are as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued was 5,884,500 silver dollars. The amount of exchange coupon reserve was 5,884,500 silver dollars. The cash reserve was 3,748,000 silver dollars. The guarantee reserve was 2,136,500 silver dollars. It was found that the cash reserve and the guarantee reserve were in line with the legal ratio. This is a special report. 24.7.13. (39-12).

Digest of Rent Reduction Movement

Zhongde Lane, Beijing Road: The Zhongde Lane branch of the 24th District Branch of the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Association held a general membership meeting yesterday. Tong Huitang was publicly elected as chairman. He reported that (1) the landlord, Mr. Fang Shu, had agreed to reduce the rent by 15% starting from July. (2) The rental contract conditions set by the landlord were too harsh in the fourth and sixth clauses, and he has voluntarily withdrawn them to avoid supplementary revisions. (3) Members' rent payments are allowed to be paid in monthly installments. (4) All previously collected miscellaneous rent items have also been voluntarily canceled. (5) Mr. Fang Shu sent written notice of rent reduction. Subsequently, discussions were held on how to express gratitude for the landlord's acceptance of the rent reduction plan. It was resolved to submit a special letter of thanks to the Municipal Federation and the Municipal Federation District Branch. Secondly, discussions were held on how to deal with the frequent gatherings of child beggars in the lane, clamoring and fighting for food, and occupying the lane. It was resolved to instruct the gatekeepers to expel them at any time. Thirdly, in response to the Municipal Party Department's order that all businesses and residents should purchase national flags and hang them uniformly for every celebration date from August onwards, it was resolved to notify all members to comply. The rest is omitted.

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong is cloudy with showers, and the wind comes from the northeast to the northwest. This is due to the passage of low pressure moving to the northeast east. The Yangtze River basin is cloudy and sultry, and there may be thunder. The breeze is non-directional. The hurricane center was approximately 120 miles within 16 degrees north latitude and 123 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM. It is moving northwest. The wind force is unknown. Letters to the Editor

To the esteemed editor of the Shenbao:

I am writing to inform you that our company has been engaged in the export of grass hats for 30 years. Our annual turnover is very large. We have made great efforts to promote domestic products and maintain small rural industries. Unfortunately, we often find it difficult to obtain raw materials for knitting hats. Except for some suitable products in the Ningbo area, we have to rely on foreign countries for everything else. We are unable to use all domestic products, which is always a regret. Our country has vast land and abundant resources. There must be many places in the mainland that produce them. However, because Chinese people are not good at publicity, we have no way of knowing anything other than the nearby areas. Therefore, our company intends to widely solicit information on the place of origin and procurement methods of raw materials for weaving straw hats (excluding wheat straw and mat grass). If anyone knows, we would be very grateful for their guidance. Please publish this in the Letters to the Editor column, so that it can reach remote areas. We are very grateful.

Respectfully,

Chuan Qilin of Kunhe Huahang

Sports News

Promulgation of National Martial Arts Rules for the National Games (1)

The rules of the National Martial Arts Competition of the Sixth National Games have been reviewed, revised and promulgated by the Competition Committee. In the future, it will be submitted to the Organizing Committee for approval. The drafting of this rule is based on the rules of the previous National Games, and at the same time, it adopts the opinions of the head of the National Martial Arts Section and several martial arts experts, and refers to the principles of general competition methods, and integrates them. It has been formed through initial drafts, research, deliberation, and repeated revisions. The draft has been changed many times in the middle before being submitted to the Competition Committee for review and approval. It has taken more than 70 hours. In terms of content, it can be called relatively complete.

The biggest change in this year's rules is that both boxing and weapons have been changed to performance competitions. According to the level of performance skills, the ranking of each person is judged. In recent times, martial arts experts have many different opinions. Some advocate competition, and some advocate performance. In fact, both methods are reasonable and have their own advantages. The National Games, in view of the provincial and municipal martial arts halls in various provinces and cities, have provincial and municipal examinations, and the central government has national examinations, all of which use competition methods to produce names and cultivate martial arts ethics. Therefore, this conference specially changed the two competitions to performances, so that the two methods can complement each other, which is not bad. Wrestling, archery, projectiles, shuttlecock kicking, and strength measurement, etc., all follow the old ones and use competition to determine the winner. However, the methods have been greatly changed and are more concrete and scientific than the rules of the previous session. The full text of the rules is nine chapters and forty-one articles.

Because of the change in the competition rules of this National Games, martial arts has been changed to one of the ordinary championships, and no longer a general championship. Therefore, the previous boxing championship, weapons championship, etc., have become one of today's events. The total number of events is 15 in the men's division and 11 in the women's division. Each event records 6 each or 6 pairs (boxing has paired boxing, and weapons also have paired weapons). They are scored at 754321, and the ranking is judged according to the total score obtained by each unit. This is also a major change in this year's rules. In addition to the wrestling and side-force events in the men's division, each is divided into heavy, middle, and light weight classes according to weight. In addition to fairness, the remaining events are generally not divided into classes. The grading standards for the above two events have also been revised. In addition, the abstract method of evaluating results for archery and projectiles and judging the ranking is now deleted and replaced with other reasonable methods. For example, the strength measurement competition also has concrete measures included in this session. Looking at the full text, the organization is clear and can be seen at a glance. However, the method used to compete for the top six places out of eight people after the wrestling elimination competition reaches the semi-finals and the week after is relatively complicated. The full text of the rules is recorded below.

National Martial Arts Competition Rules

Chapter 1: Competition Officials

Article 1: Allocation of Officials

The National Martial Arts Competition should have the following officials: (1) One Chief Referee, (2) One Deputy Referee, (3) Five to Seven Boxing Referees, (4) Five to Seven Weapons Referees, (5) Three to Five Wrestling Referees, (6) Three to Five Archery Referees, (7) Three to Nine Pellet Shooting Referees, (8) Three to Five Shuttlecock Kicking Referees, (9) Three to Five Strength Testing Referees, (10) Seven Timers, (11) Seven Recorders, (12) Seven Managers, (13) Seven Registrars, (14) One Recorder and One Assistant Recorder (Note: For all the above officials, assistant officials may be added as needed, except for the Chief Referee and the referees for each event).

Article 2: Chief Referee

The duties and powers of the Chief Referee are as follows: (1) The Chief Referee shall pay attention to the implementation of the competition rules and decide on all issues in the competition that are not detailed in the rules. (2) If the decisions of the referees are not consistent, the Chief Referee shall resolve them. The Chief Referee has the right to disqualify competitors who engage in misconduct. If protests or disputes arise regarding the conduct of competitors during the competition, the Chief Referee shall resolve them on the spot, and this decision shall be final. (3) Allocate officials for each competition event. (4) The Chief Referee has the power to order the suspension of the competition and change the competition time when necessary. (5) The Deputy Referee assists the Chief Referee in performing his duties and may act on behalf of the Chief Referee when the Chief Referee is absent.

Article 3: Referees

The duties and powers of the Referees are as follows: (1) Announce the beginning and end of each competition, observe the progress of the competition, and determine the winner. (2) Record the competition results or winners on the referee record sheet. (3) If the competition cannot be concluded due to obstruction by spectators or competitors, or due to other special circumstances, they may consult with the Chief Referee at any time to suspend the competition. (4) If a competitor disobeys the decision or order of a referee, intentionally violates the rules, or violates the rules unintentionally but is still responsible for the violation, the referee may report to the Chief Referee and order the competitor to leave the field. (5) Referees may conduct inspections of competitors at any time.

Article 4: Timers

The timer should ring the bell at the beginning and end of each competition, and sound a whistle five seconds before the start of the competition as a preparatory command.

Article 5: Recorders

The duties of the Recorder are as follows: (1) Record the progress and results of the competition. (2) Record the scores and rankings of boxing performance competitions. (3) Record the scores and rankings of weapons performance competitions. (4) Record the falls, scores, and rankings of wrestling competitions. (5) Record the number of targets hit and the number of shots, as well as the distance of archery. (6) Record the hitting of targets in pellet shooting. (7) Record the number of kicks in both plate-kicking and alternating-kicking in shuttlecock kicking competitions. (8) Record the magnitude of various forces in strength testing competitions. (9) Record violations during the competition. (10) Record the absence and forfeiture of athletes. (11) All competition results shall be signed by the referee and submitted to the Chief Recorder.

Article 6: Managers

The duties of the Manager are as follows: (1) Before and after each competition, use a command flag to direct competitors to enter and leave the field. (2) Each time a victory or defeat is determined, stand in the middle of the competitors with the command flag raised to indicate that the victory or defeat has been decided. (3) When competitors are grappling or violating the rules during the competition, stop them according to the orders of the Chief Referee or referee. (4) When an accident is about to occur during the competition, provide assistance at any time.

Article 7: Registrars

The duties of the Registrars are as follows: (1) Handle the drawing of lots. (2) Verify the weight of the competitors before the start of wrestling and strength testing competitions. If there is any discrepancy, notify the referee to handle it according to the rules. (3) Preside over the grouping matters for competitions that have rematches.

Article 8: Chief Recorder

The duties of the Chief Recorder are as follows: (1) Collect and keep the results of each competition from the recorders. (2) Announce the winners and results of each competition. (3) Calculate the scores obtained by each unit and determine their ranking.

Chapter 2: General Competition Rules

Article 9: Competition Events and Divisions

The men's competition is divided into fifteen events as follows:

Men's Division

Boxing (1) Individual (2) Pair

Weapons (3) Individual (4) Pair

Wrestling (5) Heavyweight (6) Middleweight (7) Lightweight

Archery (8) Target Shooting (9) Distance Shooting

Pellet Shooting (10) Pellet Shooting

Shuttlecock Kicking (11) Plate Kicking (12) Alternating Kicking

Strength Testing (13) Heavyweight (14) Middleweight (15) Lightweight

The women's competition is divided into eleven events as follows:

Women's Division

Boxing (1) Individual (2) Pair

Weapons (3) Individual (4) Pair

Wrestling (5) Wrestling

Archery (6) Target Shooting (7) Distance Shooting

Pellet Shooting (8) Pellet Shooting

Shuttlecock Kicking (9) Crossover Kicking

Strength Testing (11) Strength Testing

The divisions for men's wrestling and strength testing are based on the following weights: (1) Heavyweight: 81.81 kg (180 lbs) or more. (2) Middleweight: 63.63 kg (140 lbs) or more to 81.81 kg. (3) Lightweight: 63.63 kg and below. Competitors in a lighter division may voluntarily participate in a heavier division. However, if a competitor registers to participate in a lighter division, and the registrar verifies before the competition that the competitor should belong to a heavier division, the competitor will lose his qualification, unless the unit does not have enough registered competitors in the heavier division, in which case the competitor may be allowed to move up to the heavier division.

Article 10: Athlete Quota

Each unit can enter up to four people in each event in both the men's and women's divisions (four pairs for pair events). Each athlete can enter up to four events. Pair events are also counted as one event.

Article 11: Method of Calculating Championships

Six places or six pairs are awarded for each event. Their scores are calculated as 7, 5, 4, 3, 2, 1. The ranking of each unit in the men's national martial arts championship is determined by the total score obtained in the fifteen events in that division. The ranking of the women's national martial arts championship is determined by the total score obtained in the eleven events in that division.

Article 12: Forfeiture

Failure to appear at the venue after the prescribed competition time will be considered a forfeiture. If the competition is a match-up, then when one competitor forfeits, his opponent will be deemed to have won.

Article 13: Athlete Management Regulations

(1) Athletes scheduled to compete should gather at the competition venue twenty minutes before the competition.

(2) After gathering for the competition, athletes must not leave the field arbitrarily, otherwise, those who do not appear when their competition is scheduled will still be considered to have forfeited.

(3) During the competition, athletes are not allowed to make meaningless noises or make remarks that hurt the feelings of their opponents.

(4) The decisions and orders of the Chief Referee and referees must be absolutely obeyed.

(5) Those with untidy attire will be prohibited from entering the competition.

Chapter 3: Boxing and Weapons

Article 14: Competition Method

Boxing and weapons competitions use the quality of performance as a method to determine the rankings. Boxing performances, whether individual or pair, are limited to one set each time. The content of the performance is up to each person to choose, regardless of sect.

Weapons performances, whether individual or pair, are limited to one set each time. The weapons used are limited to swords, sabers, spears, and staffs. However, during a pair performance, both sides are not limited to using the same weapons.

(Note) When registering, each unit should notify the Martial Arts Division in writing of the name of the performance and the weapons used by each boxing and weapons competitor in the unit.

Article 15: Time Limit

The performance time for each person or pair is limited to five minutes. If necessary, the consent of the Chief Referee should be obtained before the competition to extend the time as appropriate.

Article 16: Judging Standards

Performance results are based on posture, movement, and energy exertion. Each type is calculated with 100 points. The average of the total scores of the three types is the score to be awarded.

During the performance, the referees will give the appropriate scores based on subjective judgment, according to the seven methods. Then, the scores evaluated by the referees in charge of this competition will be averaged. The winner of the preliminary or semi-final, and the ranking of the final, will be determined according to the average score.

Article 17: Preliminary and Final Rounds

Boxing and weapons competitions, whether individual or pair, use the group preliminary round method to eliminate some of them, and then hold the final round. If there are too many people, a semi-final may be held after the preliminary round. The grouping will be determined by the Martial Arts Division based on the participation of each unit. Each group is based on six to ten people, and the principle is to allocate athletes from each unit into different groups. The number of places to be admitted in each group in the preliminary or semi-final will be determined by the Martial Arts Division based on the number of people in each group. (To be continued)

Ministries of Industry and Education to Begin Second Phase of Work on Labor Education Experimental Zone

Based on the Labor Education Design Committee's resolution to designate five locations to establish labor education experimental zones, the Ministries of Industry and Education sent two section chiefs to Wuxi and Shanghai last year to conduct investigations and provide guidance. The labor education experimental zones in Shanghai and Wuxi have been established one after another, and the Ministries of Industry and Education have jointly hired Pan Gongzhan, et al. (Shanghai), Gao Jian Si, et al. (Wuxi) to establish labor education experimental guidance committees in Shanghai and Wuxi respectively, in order to carry out labor education in each area. In addition to these one locations, according to the original plan of the Design Committee and the two ministries, labor education experimental zones must also be established in Qingdao, Tianjin, and Hankou. Elementary and Middle Schools in the City Should Fulfill Scout Registration - City Education Bureau Specifically Orders All Schools to Comply

The Shanghai City Education Bureau instructed public and private junior high schools and elementary schools, saying that the bureau investigated that at the joint athletic meeting of elementary schools held in the eighth district this year, the scouts of Zhenru Experimental Middle School and Elementary School abandoned their duties, disturbed the order of the meeting, and had no discipline. The China Scout Association Shanghai Special City Council was informed to severely punish the matter. Subsequently, a reply was received stating, "After sending personnel to investigate, it was found that the scouts of the middle school and elementary school of Zhenru Experimental School have not fulfilled their registration, and legally do not have scout membership. The coaches in charge have also not registered and passed as service members. Our association has no right to punish them. It has been found that your bureau stipulates that scout uniforms should be used as school uniforms for all schools in the city, causing the uniforms of genuine scouts and students to be the same, making it difficult to distinguish them. Therefore, in order to avoid similar situations from happening in the future, our association believes that your bureau should issue a notice to all schools in the city that use scout uniforms as school uniforms to implement training and register, and training personnel must also register with our association and obtain service member qualifications before they can be in charge. Then our association can be supervised in accordance with legal regulations." In addition, the bureau announced the Shanghai Primary and Secondary School Student Uniform Unification Method, stipulating that the classes of junior high school students and graduates who implement scout training should use scout uniforms as uniforms. All schools should earnestly implement scout training and register in accordance with the regulations, and hire registered and qualified personnel as coaches to command. In addition to ordering Zhenru Experimental Middle School to earnestly comply, all junior high schools and elementary schools in the city that have not completed scout registration procedures and whose hired coaches have not registered and passed, should complete these procedures immediately. Do not delay. This order must be followed.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Etiquette (Short Lecture Platform)

— Kang Jianzhai

We Chinese, have historically called ourselves a nation of propriety and righteousness. Now, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek is promoting the New Life Movement, and the first thing he emphasizes is this word "etiquette."

Humans are educated animals. Having received education, one must understand etiquette. A person who does not understand etiquette, even if talented, will not be able to do well in society. A nation that does not value propriety and righteousness, even if wealthy and powerful, cannot maintain world peace.

Three thousand years ago, we had an ancient poem: "Look at the rat, it has skin; a man without etiquette. A man without etiquette, why not die quickly!" To put it in modern language, it means: "Look, even rats have fur and skin, how can a person be without etiquette? If a person has no etiquette, why not hasten their own death!"

Why does a lack of etiquette lead to death? Confucius said, "Valor without etiquette leads to chaos." Individual treason and rebellion, national invasion of the weak, and a one-sided pursuit of military strength – such individuals and such nations will either commit suicide or be killed in the end. Isn't that hastening one's own death?

These words are too broad. Here, we will only discuss from the perspective of the individual: what is called etiquette?

To understand the etiquette of being a person, one must learn good manners. To have good manners, one must possess three inner elements: "harmony," "humility," and "sincerity."

To put it simply: everyone must treat each other with love, affection, and sincerity. With sincerity inside, good manners will naturally be displayed on the outside. (Current Affairs Research)

The Great Flood is Here Again (Current Affairs Research)

— He Gongchao

Children, the great flood is here again! These past few days, the newspapers have been reporting every day: Hankou, Nanjing, Anhui, Jiangxi, Kaifeng, and Guangzhou are all experiencing severe floods. Some villages have been completely washed away by the flood, and in some cities, the water has already entered the streets. Who would have thought that just four years after the great flood of 1931, it would happen again!

Recalling the flood that year, sixteen provinces were affected, and the loss of property and lives was immeasurable. Are we, the Chinese people, going to suffer again this year?

Some people say, "This is a natural disaster. Heaven wants us to suffer, and there's nothing we can do about it." But, children, we must think about it: Is this really something we can't do anything about? We must know that European and American countries used to experience frequent floods as well, but later they used science to dredge rivers and increase forests, and in recent years, we haven't heard much about floods. However, in China, just during the Qing Dynasty, there were more than two hundred major floods. Since the founding of the Republic, there have been three or four major floods, and even more minor floods. Is this because there's nothing we can do, or because we're unwilling to find a solution and unwilling to implement good solutions?

The severity of floods surpasses that of fires by tens of thousands of times. Please see the following account:

"In Wuyuan (a county in Anhui Province), on the 25th and 27th, it rained torrentially day and night. The mountain floods burst forth, as if the earth had cracked and the mountains had collapsed. Water shot straight up from the ground for tens of feet, and white waves chased each other like columns of silver reaching for the sky. Large rocks and logs from the mountains rushed down with the water, and in the blink of an eye, hundreds of miles of farmland were piled high with sand and stones. Corpses floated here and there in the waves. The entire county was a vast expanse of water, completely transformed into a water kingdom..."

Children, after reading this account, how do you feel?

Children, in this era of great disaster, I believe we should do the following things: (1) Research the causes of floods and methods of prevention. (2) Save your candy money to help the refugees. (3) Prepare to participate in fundraising and disaster relief efforts.

What do you think?

The red sun sets,

The sky has cleared,

As if saying:

May you grow up,

"Save the nation!" "Save the people!"

Summer Clothes (Common Sense)

— Rong

One Saturday afternoon, Min'er and Cong'er went for a walk on the street. They saw everyone on the street wearing white clothes. Min'er was very curious and asked his brother Cong'er, "Why are they all wearing white clothes now?" Cong'er replied, "Min'er, it's because the weather is very hot in the summer. White clothes can reflect sunlight, while black clothes can absorb sunlight. It's cooler to wear white clothes." Min'er asked doubtfully, "Brother Cong, I don't quite believe it. Can you demonstrate it for me?" Cong'er said, "Min'er, if you don't believe it, I'll demonstrate it for you when we get home." Min'er, hearing about the demonstration, didn't want to see anything else and kept urging his brother to go home quickly. Cong'er said, "Min'er, it's still early. Why are you in such a hurry to go home?" Min'er said, "Brother Cong, I'm in a hurry to go home so I can see your demonstration!" Cong'er said, "I see. Then let me buy some supplies for the demonstration." As he spoke, he reached into his pocket and bought five copper coins worth of ice cream on Bingtan Street, and then hurried home with his brother.

Soon, they arrived home. Cong'er prepared a piece of white cloth and a piece of black cloth. Min'er looked at the two pieces of ice cream they had just bought and didn't understand. He asked his brother again, "What are these things for?" Cong'er replied to his brother, "Just watch and you'll know." Cong'er wrapped a piece of ice cream in the white cloth and a piece of ice cream in the black cloth and put them in the sun. Soon, the ice cream wrapped in the black cloth melted quickly, while the ice cream wrapped in the white cloth melted very slowly. Cong'er said, "Min'er, now you know. Wearing white clothes in the summer reflects sunlight and reduces heat, while wearing black clothes in the winter absorbs sunlight, so you feel warmer."

The Plain and the Mountain (Fable)

— Gong Wang

The plain said to the mountain, "Sir, may I ask, what use are you in the world? I see your bare head and your high brow reaching into the clouds, and I have never seen your purpose..."

The mountain said, "Sir, then please tell me, what use are you?"

"Don't you know my use? Don't you see that I produce grains, sugar, wheat, etc. to supply people's needs? Countless cattle and sheep eat the green grass that grows on my chest. Rain falls on me, and large rivers and small streams come to moisten me. People store my products, and boats can travel across the rivers to all corners of the world. How can you say I have no use?"

The mountain said, "Sir, I won't argue with you, but you cannot do without me. Every blade of grass and every leaf of yours needs my water to irrigate it. Without me, the large rivers and small streams would dry up, and the flowers and trees would not be able to survive. You would become a desert..."

Children's Science Lecture: The Flower of a Plant

— Lin Yin

The flower is an important part of the plant, and the flower of a flowering plant is even more so, it is its lifeline. If there were no flowers, it would never reproduce. A flower, as we see it, seems to be very simple. Some children like it very much and pluck it off, but in the plant itself, it is losing a part of its life. Each flower can be roughly divided into four parts (Figure 1). The names of the four parts are: calyx, corolla, stamen, pistil. The calyx is green and is the outermost part of the corolla. Its shape is varied, some like tubes, some like funnels, some like lips, and some like pots (Figure 2). It mostly falls off when flowering, but some fall off at the same time as the corolla. It protects the flower buds. The shape of the corolla is even more varied, depending on the type of plant. There are bell shapes, lip shapes, tongue shapes, wing shapes, and butterfly shapes (Figure 3). Inside the corolla, there are slender filaments with anthers at the upper end, called stamens. There are many stamens. Surrounded by many stamens, there is a thicker style with an ovary at the lower end, a stigma at the upper end, and ovules in the middle (Figure 4). When the ovules in this stigma combine with the pollen on the upper end of the pistil, fruits will be produced, and fruits are the lifeline of plant reproduction. This combination of pollen and ovules is sometimes aided by insects, such as peach blossoms, plum blossoms, and pear blossoms. These flowers have colors and fragrances, and also secrete nectar to attract insects to transmit pollen for them and produce fruit. Such flowers are called entomophilous flowers (Figure 5). Another type of flower uses wind power to spread pollen. They have no color, no fragrance, and no sweetness, so insects will not gather pollen. Examples of such flowers include rice, wheat, and dandelions. These are called anemophilous flowers (Figure 6).

How to Organize a Summer Reading Group? (Research)

— Shen Chengzhao

Dear children, how quickly time flies! In the blink of an eye, the annual summer vacation has arrived again.

Are we going to just play and let the precious time slip away during the nearly two-month-long summer vacation? Are we going to forget the books we read at school and return them to the teacher? No, definitely not! We should find a way to not only remember the books we've read, but also add some knowledge to our minds.

The best way is to immediately organize a summer reading group. Reading is more interesting when it is organized.

As for the method of organizing a summer reading group, please see the left:

(1) Gather three to five people as basic members, responsible for borrowing books, returning books, convening meetings, and evaluating the work of members.

(2) Ordinary members, ten to twenty people, with every five people making up a group. Everyone discusses and decides on the books to be read in each group. Then, the time, amount, and deadline are also discussed and agreed upon in advance. After reading, everyone gathers again, and each member reports on the interest and insights gained from reading.

(3) Each group also has competitions. Which group reads the most books, which group reports the most clearly, and which group does the worst. The basic members will evaluate.

(4) Difficulties that are not understood can be raised for discussion.

(5) Tea party once a week. (Time and venue are determined by the group)

(6) Each member contributes two dimes. (For purchasing books, newspapers, tea, and refreshments)

Alright, time is precious, children, let's get up and do it!

Children's Corner

A Visit to a New German Mail Ship

— Lin Dianyi, Third Grader of Shanghai Xiejin Elementary School

At 10 AM on June 27th, my fourth uncle and second brother came by car to pick up my father, sisters, and me to visit the Norddeutscher Lloyd's new mail ship, the Scharnhorst, at the Gonghexiang Wharf. When we got on the ship, we saw cranes lifting various goods from the cargo hold, some onto barges and some onto the dock. We visited various rooms, and the facilities were clean and magnificent. There was also a children's play area, and two open-air swimming pools on the deck. Then we went to the captain's quarters, stood next to the compass with my sisters, and my second brother took a picture of us to commemorate the occasion. Later, we went to the reception room and saw two oil paintings. One was of the famous World War I general and German President Hindenburg, who had already passed away, and the other was of the successor Head of State Hitler. They are both German national heroes who defended the country and resisted foreign insults, worthy of commemoration and worship. I hope our country can also produce more heroes of this kind. After the visit, it was already 12 o'clock, so we took the car home.

A Wishful Thinking (Indian Fairy Tale)

— Yue Qi

In a certain town, there lived a weaver. One day, the wooden pegs on his loom broke. He took an ax and ran outside to look for wood. He ran to the beach and saw a large Bodhi tree. He thought to himself, "This tree looks good. If I cut it down, I can make many parts for the loom." As he thought this, he raised his ax and chopped at it.

At that moment, a fairy living in the big tree came out and said, "Friend, this tree is my home. I live here very happily. Please spare it."

"But, sir," the weaver replied, "sparing your home means starving my family, because the loom that feeds my family is now missing pegs. So, please move somewhere else, and quickly. I'm going to cut down this tree."

The fairy said, "Sir, since that's the case, I'll give you whatever you want, as long as you spare this tree."

"Then," the weaver said, "let me go back and ask my friend and my wife." The fairy agreed, and the weaver set off for home. On the way to the town, he met his friend, the barber! He said, "Friend, the fairy promised me that he would give me whatever I want. Tell me what I should ask for."

The barber replied, "Friend, if that's really the case, then ask for a kingdom! You can be the emperor, and I can be the prime minister. Is there anything better than that in the world?"

The weaver returned home and said to his wife, "Dear wife, today a fairy promised me that he would give me whatever I want. Think about it, what should I ask for? My friend, the barber, told me to ask for a kingdom."

"Dear husband," the wife said, "don't listen to the barber. Being a king is the most troublesome and unsafe thing. Ask for something else instead."

"What something else, you say?"

"Before, you wove a bolt of cloth every day, enough for us to spend for one day. Now, go and ask for another head and two more arms. Then you can weave a bolt of cloth in front and a bolt of cloth in back every day. One bolt of cloth is enough for us to spend for one day, and you can save the money from the other bolt of cloth for a better life in the future."

The weaver was very happy and said, "That's a good idea. I've decided to listen to you."

The weaver went to the fairy and explained his request: "Fairy, please give me a second head and second pair of arms." As soon as he finished speaking, he became a man with two heads and four arms.

The weaver walked home, feeling very happy. When the people saw him, they thought he was a monster. Everyone beat him with sticks and threw stones at him. He died on the road, leaving behind a broken loom at home.

Readers please note: The Chinese Children's Culture Association will be broadcasting today from 12 PM to 1 PM at the Xinxin Radio Station (frequency 780). Mr. He Gongchao will be speaking on "How to Be a Modern Child." Mr. Zhang Youjian will be telling the story of "Sacrifice for the Tree." The children's choir organized by the association will be broadcasting songs. Children are asked to tune in at that time. Also, the association is currently recruiting male, female, and child members. Those who wish to join can write to the association at No. 457, 2nd Floor, Henan Road, to request the regulations.

The Adventures of Sinbad the Sailor (26)

— Xin Qing

For a long time I continued in this hunting sport, every day an elephant fell by my bow; one day, as I was watching the beasts from the tree, I saw a great herd appear. The earth shook because of them, and the sounds they made filled me with fear.

They surrounded the tree I sat upon, their little black eyes constantly fixed on me; they gave me such a fright that my bow fell from my hand.

A great beast came near the tree, twisted its trunk with its trunk, and tugged hard; and the tree was uprooted and thrown to the ground.

Of course, I fell with the tree. The elephant came to me, and with his trunk, rolled me up and placed me on his back. I knew not what would happen, and lay as if half dead.

Then the whole herd went with me, until they came to a distant place; then I was placed upon the ground.

Thereupon they left me and went away. As soon as I was sure that they were all gone, I struggled to rise; and found myself upon a great mountain, scattered over with the bones and tusks of dead elephants.

I then comprehended wherefore the beasts had brought me to this place, they knew that I killed them for their teeth and thought that if I knew these bones, I would stop killing them.

I did not delay, but immediately set out for the town. I arrived there and sought the man who had bought me, and told him my news.

He rejoiced to see me, for he had been in the forest, and had seen my bow lying near to a tree that had been uprooted. Seeing these things, he thought that the beasts had killed me.

I told him all that had happened to me, and what I had seen on the mountain. The next day we went out together and obtained a great quantity of ivory.

After we went back, he said: "Sinbad, I will not treat you like a slave any longer, you are free. I will tell you why. Although I did not tell you before, the elephants in those forests killed many slaves, like you sent to kill them because of their teeth. You were not hurt, which shows that God is watching over you, so the beasts could not harm you. What you found on the mountain gave me a great fortune! I will give you your freedom and make you rich."

Hearing this, I hastened to say: "My lord, may God watch over you. I do not want wealth; now that I am free, I wish to leave this place and return to my home."

He said: "So that you may do so, I will pay you all the expenses of the voyage. Soon there will be ships coming to buy all our ivory, and you can take one of them to go home."

I had to stay with him for a few days, waiting for the time when the ships would come.

Financials Gold Prices Rise, Foreign Banks Retrench, Benefiting Bulls, Standard Gold Price Exceeds Forty Dollars

—Midday Increase of Ten Dollars and Four Cents—

Yesterday, the gold market saw overseas silver markets suddenly announce declines, with extremely weak support. Market sentiment was stimulated, leading to a surge in buying that pushed prices beyond the forty-dollar mark. Due to swap transactions, the market conditions for half the day were particularly mediocre, with insignificant fluctuations. The morning began with overseas silver markets retracting, and major support levels reported weakness. The final transaction price after the market closed continued to drop by 1.25. The forward silver price in Montreaux also fell by between 7.5 and 1.25 fen. Exchange rates slightly contracted, and the price of London raw gold rose by three pence. Market sentiment was quite bullish, and pre-market trading opened, immediately rising to thirty-eight or thirty-nine dollars. There was a shortage of sellers, and soon the price rose further to over forty-two dollars. The Central Bank's official rates were announced, with English and American rates remaining unchanged. The Customs Gold Unit rose by three li, and the standard gold price was posted at $868.80. Afterwards, it turned to range trading and settled down, but once retreated to the forty-dollar mark. However, due to renewed strong buying interest, it soon rose again. Qiao Zhifu of the Dog Tai firm and HSBC were willing to release shillings, and sellers were still active, gradually pushing the price down. HSBC's posted rates also remained unchanged. Despite this, market sentiment was quite strong, and buyers took advantage of the dips to maintain their positions. In addition, the Hong Kong market softened, making it easier to rebound. Although banks were unwilling to increase their holdings, British American Tobacco continued to buy US dollars, keeping the Hong Kong market tight. Reuters reported that Indian silver was expected to fall by three annas, stabilizing the situation. Although there was a slight setback at the end due to Hong Kong market easing by 0.0625 and support levels reporting strength, buying interest was strong, and the midday market remained bullish. Prices continued to rise after the market closed, and the overall trend for the day was robust. The rollover trading for August and September will begin on Monday, and it is predicted that the short side will still need to cover, but the level of the premium will depend on the strength of both sides. Qiao Zhifu covered August shillings at 0.75, falling to 0.06. Hengyu, Fuxing Yong took delivery, rising to $3.90. Yifeng Yongyi Cheng still sold at $1.50. The Hong Kong market softened, Fuxing Yong, Huixiang Chunyuan Yong, Fuyu, and Tongyi jointly took delivery, briefly rallying to $5. Shanghai Datong covered September shillings at 5.5625. Yifeng Yong Tongyu Run Hengyu took advantage of the high prices to sell, falling to $2.30. Fuxing Yong still maintained its position, rising to $3.30. Foodstuffs - Flour and Wheat Plunge Sharply Again

The flour market saw another sharp drop yesterday. Quotations for foreign wheat from Chicago fell around 5-6 jiao, and from Canada fell 1 jiao. The market sentiment was unanimously cautious, mainly because the domestic economy is in a state of contraction, and the purchasing power of both the public and private sectors is naturally weak. This year's Yangtze River disaster area is both severe and large, and there should be some pull from that, but there is no movement at present. Overseas trends are also unfavorable, so opening prices were weak. By the afternoon, market sentiment for near-term deliveries became even more fearful because actual sales were sluggish. Bulls had no choice but to unwind their positions, and the decline was therefore sharp. It was reported that factories and trading houses placed orders for foreign wheat for far-term deliveries at prices between 4.40 and 4.41 yuan, so sellers switched to dropping prices without end. As a result, the current month fell by as much as 3 fen, August fell 3 fen, September fell 2.5 fen, October fell 2.25 fen, November fell 2 fen, and December fell 1.5 fen, it was said.

The wheat market was uniformly weak yesterday because quotations for foreign wheat continued to fall, and the selling of spot wheat was incessant. Moreover, domestic new wheat had just entered the market, and this phenomenon already exists. It is naturally more difficult to imagine what will happen later. The silence of buyers has a reason. There were spot wheat hedges for near-term deliveries and foreign wheat hedges for far-term deliveries, so bid prices uniformly loosened. As a result, the current month fell 3 fen, August fell 3 fen, September and October fell 4 fen, and November fell 7 fen. Trading houses directly supplied about 1,000 bags of spot wheat to factories at prices of 3.27-3.35 yuan, but the guild market did not officially list it, it was said.

Rice Prices Fall Again Due to Hot and Sunny Weather

Local rice: Yesterday, the total arrival of goods from various sources in Shanghai South was 23-24 batches (totaling 4,700-4,800 shi). The downward trend was particularly fierce, with a drastic drop. Sales of various thick japonica and thin indica rices continued to be sluggish, and market quotations plummeted again by 0.10-0.40 yuan. Only the Qingdao firm bought over a hundred bags. Yinlian yuan was negatively affected. In Shanghai North, 18-19 boats arrived from various river areas yesterday. Various goods in the market were moving slowly. White japonica rice saw a slight improvement with price reductions, with high-grade rice down 0.20 yuan and medium-grade rice down 0.30-0.40 yuan. Early thin indica rice sales were also sluggish, with prices down 0.20-0.30 yuan. White yuan sales remained sluggish, and prices fell slightly again. The prices of other goods also fell by about 0.10 yuan.

Regarding the foreign rice market situation, although sales along the Yangtze River were active, the situation continued to show softness. After the hot weather, many river rice sellers were eager to sell off their stock, and medium-grade foreign rice sellers were also very eager to sell. High-grade foreign rice had arrived, and the market already showed signs of weakness. Yesterday, sales along the Yangtze River decreased slightly, and the local market was even more quiet, with very tight price controls for immediate needs. Therefore, high and medium-grade rice prices generally softened. However, due to the serious flooding along the Yangtze River, there will definitely be a need for smooth operations in the future, so prices were able to hold. Yesterday, a total of 7,000 bags of Western-bought rice were sold, including high-grade gongmi, small jiaomi, Su japonica, and Siamese rice, with prices similar to the previous market.

Yesterday, soybean cake market prices fell by 0.07-0.08 yuan in one day. Even if there were scattered sales, it was like finding treasure. So, the sales volume reached over 10,000 pieces. Sales of soybeans were only slightly active in the local market.

Metals - Pig Lead and Iron Prices Fall by Over One Yuan

Recent transactions in pig lead and iron have been sluggish because toy factories have stopped procurement. The market situation is very stagnant. Black Iron Sheet After the Off-Season

Northern and Southern Goods - Xiang Lotus Seeds Report Crop Failure Due to Flooding

Hankou-Shanghai Market Prices Tight

Yesterday, according to a letter from Hankou, the Xiangxi region's harvest of Xiang lotus seeds is bound to be poor due to flooding, and the source of supply has been disrupted. The market situation suddenly tightened. Therefore, sales in the local market increased by 3 yuan or more. For example, new Jiu Xi lotus seeds in the shell were quoted at 33-34 yuan, and old goods followed closely. However, the inventory of various firms was already not thick, and most of it was stored in cold storage warehouses. Now, hearing this news, there is even more certainty about future price increases. The resolve to hold on is becoming stronger. There is hope that high-quality goods will reach 46-47 yuan in the future. Yesterday, according to a telegram from Hankou, new tree ears were disrupted by flood in their source so the shipment stopped, and local prices rose. The price was 86-87 yuan, or perhaps nearly 90 yuan. The local market price for top-grade Air Mail small-package tree ears is still 105-106 yuan; other items are the same. The future market may follow the tightening trend.

Oil Market - Reasons for the Sudden Rise and Fall of Asphalt

Asphalt sales are usually in the off-season during the summer. However, with the rise of soap factories, most of their raw materials are taken from asphalt. Therefore, asphalt usage for soap-making is more than for candle-making. It is precisely during the period when candle production is suspended in the summer that factories are actively using asphalt. Moreover, since soap usage is greater than candle usage, summer sales are always more brisk than winter sales. Therefore, for the past ten years or so, there has been no real off-season. Supply and demand are well balanced. However, the situation has suddenly changed in the past three or four years. Soap-making now almost exclusively uses foreign products such as coconut oil and tallow, and asphalt soap-making has reached its limit. Therefore, every summer, it reverts to the previous off-season situation. This year's summer sales will be no exception. Since entering summer, sales have been quiet. Fortunately, inventories everywhere are low, so even though sales are light, they will not plummet. Last week, because there had been no transactions for a long time in the Hankou market, Chongjing oil fell to 11.7-11.8 taels, and Macheng oil fell to 11.4 taels. However, after the price drop, various firms in Hankou believed that the opportunity had arrived and wanted to make purchases. But the reason for the price drop in Hankou was that there had been no transactions for a long time. It was intended to stimulate the market and not because of abundant inventory. Seeing that various firms were interested in buying, the market turned around again. According to details in yesterday's letter from Hankou, there was not much Macheng oil available at 12 taels. It can be seen that last week's price drop was not a formal market event. The prices rose and fell quickly. In short, although sales are light, inventories are very low, so the market seems weak. However, as soon as there is a transaction, prices can easily rise. Local firms have very thin inventories and are not paying attention to procurement because sales are slow. Seeing that prices in Hankou had fallen slightly this time, they had also telegraphed orders, but after seeing the prices rise again, they stopped. Market quotations are still inconsistent. Approximately, Chongjing oil prices are very low, around 20 yuan per dan, it was said.
